<script>
    // Click to enlarge license image
    document.querySelectorAll('.license-image').forEach(img => {
        img.addEventListener('click', function() {
            const modal = document.createElement('div');
            modal.style.position = 'fixed';
            modal.style.top = '0';
            modal.style.left = '0';
            modal.style.width = '100%';
            modal.style.height = '100%';
            modal.style.backgroundColor = 'rgba(0,0,0,0.9)';
            modal.style.zIndex = '9999';
            modal.style.display = 'flex';
            modal.style.alignItems = 'center';
            modal.style.justifyContent = 'center';
            modal.style.cursor = 'pointer';
            
            const enlargedImg = document.createElement('img');
            enlargedImg.src = this.src;
            enlargedImg.style.maxWidth = '90%';
            enlargedImg.style.maxHeight = '90%';
            enlargedImg.style.borderRadius = '0.5rem';
            
            modal.appendChild(enlargedImg);
            modal.addEventListener('click', () => modal.remove());
            document.body.appendChild(modal);
        });
    });
</script>

--- Views/Admin/RiderApprovals.cshtml ---
<!-- Views/Admin/RiderApprovals.cshtml -->
@model IReadOnlyList<ThriftLoop.Models.Rider>
@{
    ViewData["Title"] = "Rider Approvals";
    Layout = "~/Views/Shared/_Layout.cshtml";
    var statusFilter = Context.Request.Query["status"].ToString();
}

<div class="admin-approvals">
    <div class="admin-header">
        <div>
            <h1>Rider Approvals</h1>
            <p>Review and process rider applications</p>
        </div>
    </div>

    <!-- Status Filters -->
    <div class="filter-tabs">
        <a asp-action="RiderApprovals" asp-route-status="" class="filter-tab @(string.IsNullOrEmpty(statusFilter) ? "active" : "")">All</a>
        <a asp-action="RiderApprovals" asp-route-status="pending" class="filter-tab @(statusFilter == "pending" ? "active" : "")">Pending</a>
        <a asp-action="RiderApprovals" asp-route-status="approved" class="filter-tab @(statusFilter == "approved" ? "active" : "")">Approved</a>
        <a asp-action="RiderApprovals" asp-route-status="rejected" class="filter-tab @(statusFilter == "rejected" ? "active" : "")">Rejected</a>
        <a asp-action="RiderApprovals" asp-route-status="resubmitted" class="filter-tab @(statusFilter == "resubmitted" ? "active" : "")">Resubmitted</a>
    </div>

    <!-- Riders Table -->
    <div class="table-container">
        <table class="admin-table">
            <thead>
                <tr>
                    <th>ID</th>
                    <th>Full Name</th>
                    <th>Email</th>
                    <th>Phone</th>
                    <th>Vehicle</th>
                    <th>Applied</th>
                    <th>Last Activity</th>
                    <th>Status</th>
                    <th>Actions</th>
                </tr>
            </thead>
            <tbody>
                @foreach (var rider in Model)
                {
                    // Determine status text and class
                    string statusText;
                    string statusClass;
                    bool isResubmitted = false;
                    
                    if (rider.IsApproved)
                    {
                        statusText = "Approved";
                        statusClass = "status-approved";
                    }
                    else if (!string.IsNullOrEmpty(rider.RejectionReason))
                    {
                        if (rider.ResubmittedAt.HasValue)
                        {
                            statusText = "Resubmitted";
                            statusClass = "status-resubmitted";
                            isResubmitted = true;
                        }
                        else
                        {
                            statusText = "Rejected";
                            statusClass = "status-rejected";
                        }
                    }
                    else
                    {
                        statusText = "Pending";
                        statusClass = "status-pending";
                    }
                    
                    // Determine last activity date
                    DateTime? lastActivity = rider.ResubmittedAt ?? rider.RejectedAt ?? rider.UpdatedAt;
                    
                    <tr>
                        <td>@rider.Id</td>
                        <td>@(rider.FullName ?? "—")</td>
                        <td>@rider.Email</td>
                        <td>@(rider.PhoneNumber ?? "—")</td>
                        <td>@(rider.VehicleType ?? "—")</td>
                        <td>@rider.CreatedAt.ToString("yyyy-MM-dd")</td>
                        <td>
                            @if (lastActivity.HasValue)
                            {
                                <span title="Last activity: @lastActivity.Value.ToString("yyyy-MM-dd HH:mm")">
                                    @lastActivity.Value.ToString("yyyy-MM-dd")
                                    @if (isResubmitted)
                                    {
                                        <span class="resubmit-badge" title="Resubmitted">↻</span>
                                    }
                                    else if (rider.RejectedAt.HasValue && !isResubmitted)
                                    {
                                        <span class="rejected-badge" title="Rejected">✗</span>
                                    }
                                </span>
                            }
                            else
                            {
                                <span class="text-muted">—</span>
                            }
                         </td>
                        <td>
                            <div class="status-container">
                                <span class="status-badge @statusClass">@statusText</span>
                                @if (!string.IsNullOrEmpty(rider.RejectionReason))
                                {
                                    <div class="rejection-tooltip" data-reason="@rider.RejectionReason">
                                        <svg viewBox="0 0 20 20" fill="currentColor" width="14" height="14">
                                            <path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M18 10a8 8 0 11-16 0 8 8 0 0116 0zm-7-4a1 1 0 11-2 0 1 1 0 012 0zM9 9a1 1 0 000 2v3a1 1 0 001 1h1a1 1 0 100-2v-3a1 1 0 00-1-1H9z" clip-rule="evenodd" />
                                        </svg>
                                    </div>
                                }
                            </div>
                         </td>
                        <td>
                            <div class="action-group">
                                <a asp-action="RiderApplicationDetail" asp-route-id="@rider.Id" class="action-btn btn-view">View Details</a>
                                
                                @if (!rider.IsApproved)
                                {
                                    <form method="post" asp-action="ApproveRider" class="inline-form">
                                        @Html.AntiForgeryToken()
                                        <input type="hidden" name="riderId" value="@rider.Id" />
                                        <button type="submit" class="action-btn btn-approve" onclick="return confirm('Approve rider @(rider.FullName ?? rider.Email)?')">Approve</button>
                                    </form>
                                    
                                    @if (string.IsNullOrEmpty(rider.RejectionReason))
                                    {
                                        <a asp-action="RejectRiderWithReason" asp-route-id="@rider.Id" class="action-btn btn-reject">Reject</a>
                                    }
                                    else
                                    {
                                        <a asp-action="RejectRiderWithReason" asp-route-id="@rider.Id" class="action-btn btn-reject">Re-Reject</a>
                                    }
                                }
                                else
                                {
                                    <span class="action-disabled">Approved</span>
                                }
                            </div>
                         </td>
                     </tr>
                }
            </tbody>
        </table>
    </div>

    @if (!Model.Any())
    {
        <div class="empty-state">
            <p>No rider applications found.</p>
        </div>
    }
</div>

    }

        display: inline-flex;

        color: #6b7280;
    }
    
    .rejection-tooltip:hover {
        color: #dc2626;
    }

<script>
    // Tooltip functionality for rejection reasons
    (function() {
        let activeTooltip = null;
        
        document.querySelectorAll('.rejection-tooltip').forEach(tooltip => {
            tooltip.addEventListener('mouseenter', function(e) {
                const reason = this.getAttribute('data-reason');
                if (!reason) return;
                
                // Remove any existing tooltip
                if (activeTooltip) activeTooltip.remove();
                
                // Create tooltip
                const tooltipDiv = document.createElement('div');
                tooltipDiv.className = 'rejection-custom-tooltip';
                tooltipDiv.innerHTML = `
                    <div class="tooltip-arrow"></div>
                    <div class="tooltip-content">${escapeHtml(reason)}</div>
                `;
                
                // Style the tooltip
                tooltipDiv.style.position = 'fixed';
                tooltipDiv.style.backgroundColor = '#1f2937';
                tooltipDiv.style.color = 'white';
                tooltipDiv.style.borderRadius = '0.5rem';
                tooltipDiv.style.fontSize = '0.75rem';
                tooltipDiv.style.maxWidth = '350px';
                tooltipDiv.style.zIndex = '10000';
                tooltipDiv.style.boxShadow = '0 4px 6px -1px rgba(0,0,0,0.1)';
                tooltipDiv.style.pointerEvents = 'none';
                
                const rect = this.getBoundingClientRect();
                tooltipDiv.style.bottom = (window.innerHeight - rect.top + 8) + 'px';
                tooltipDiv.style.left = rect.left + 'px';
                
                document.body.appendChild(tooltipDiv);
                activeTooltip = tooltipDiv;
            });
            
            tooltip.addEventListener('mouseleave', function() {
                if (activeTooltip) {
                    activeTooltip.remove();
                    activeTooltip = null;
                }
            });
        });
        
        // Helper function to escape HTML
        function escapeHtml(text) {
            const div = document.createElement('div');
            div.textContent = text;
            return div.innerHTML;
        }
        
        // Close tooltip on scroll
        window.addEventListener('scroll', function() {
            if (activeTooltip) {
                activeTooltip.remove();
                activeTooltip = null;
            }
        });
    })();
</script>

<style>
    /* Additional styles for custom tooltip */
    .rejection-custom-tooltip {
        position: fixed;
        background-color: #1f2937;
        color: white;
        border-radius: 0.5rem;
        font-size: 0.75rem;
        max-width: 350px;
        z-index: 10000;
        box-shadow: 0 4px 6px -1px rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.1);
        pointer-events: none;
    }
    
    .rejection-custom-tooltip .tooltip-content {
        padding: 0.5rem 0.75rem;
        word-wrap: break-word;
        line-height: 1.4;
    }
    
    .rejection-custom-tooltip .tooltip-arrow {
        position: absolute;
        bottom: -6px;
        left: 12px;
        width: 12px;
        height: 6px;
        background-color: #1f2937;
        clip-path: polygon(0% 0%, 100% 0%, 50% 100%);
    }
</style>

@model IReadOnlyList<ThriftLoop.Models.SellerProfile>
@using ThriftLoop.Enums
@{
    ViewData["Title"] = "Seller Approvals";
    Layout = "~/Views/Shared/_Layout.cshtml";
    var statusFilter = Context.Request.Query["status"].ToString();
}

<div class="admin-approvals">
    <div class="admin-header">
        <div>
            <h1>Seller Approvals</h1>
            <p>Review and process seller applications</p>
        </div>
    </div>

    <!-- Status Filters -->
    <div class="filter-tabs">
        <a asp-action="SellerApprovals" asp-route-status="" class="filter-tab @(string.IsNullOrEmpty(statusFilter) ? "active" : "")">All</a>
        <a asp-action="SellerApprovals" asp-route-status="Pending" class="filter-tab @(statusFilter == "Pending" ? "active" : "")">Pending</a>
        <a asp-action="SellerApprovals" asp-route-status="Approved" class="filter-tab @(statusFilter == "Approved" ? "active" : "")">Approved</a>
        <a asp-action="SellerApprovals" asp-route-status="Rejected" class="filter-tab @(statusFilter == "Rejected" ? "active" : "")">Rejected</a>
    </div>

    <!-- Applications Table -->
    <div class="table-container">
        <table class="admin-table">
            <thead>
                <tr>
                    <th>ID</th>
                    <th>User</th>
                    <th>Shop Name</th>
                    <th>Bio</th>
                    <th>Applied</th>
                    <th>Status</th>
                    <th>Actions</th>
                </tr>
            </thead>
            <tbody>
                @foreach (var app in Model)
                {
                    <tr>
                        <td>@app.Id</td>
                        <td>@app.User?.Email</td>
                        <td>@app.ShopName</td>
                        <td class="truncate">@(app.Bio ?? "—")</td>
                        <td>@app.AppliedAt.ToString("yyyy-MM-dd")</td>
                        <td>
                            <span class="status-badge status-@app.ApplicationStatus.ToString().ToLower()">@app.ApplicationStatus</span>
                        </td>
                        <td>
                            @if (app.ApplicationStatus == ApplicationStatus.Pending)
                            {
                                <div class="action-group">
                                    <form method="post" asp-action="ApproveSeller" class="inline-form">
                                        @Html.AntiForgeryToken()
                                        <input type="hidden" name="applicationId" value="@app.Id" />
                                        <button type="submit" class="action-btn btn-approve" onclick="return confirm('Approve @app.ShopName?')">Approve</button>
                                    </form>
                                    <form method="post" asp-action="RejectSeller" class="inline-form">
                                        @Html.AntiForgeryToken()
                                        <input type="hidden" name="applicationId" value="@app.Id" />
                                        <button type="submit" class="action-btn btn-reject" onclick="return confirm('Reject @app.ShopName?')">Reject</button>
                                    </form>
                                </div>
                            }
                            else
                            {
                                <span class="action-disabled">@(app.ApplicationStatus == ApplicationStatus.Approved ? "Approved" : "Rejected")</span>
                            }
                        </td>
                    </tr>
                }
            </tbody>
        </table>
    </div>

    @if (!Model.Any())
    {
        <div class="empty-state">
            <p>No seller applications found.</p>
        </div>
    }
</div>

        </div>
        <div class="admin-stats-badge">@Model.TotalCount total users</div>
    </div>

    <!-- Filters -->
    <form method="get" asp-action="Users" class="filter-form">
        <div class="filter-row">
            <input type="text" name="search" placeholder="Search by email..." value="@Model.SearchTerm" class="filter-input" />
            <select name="role" class="filter-select">
                <option value="">All Roles</option>
                @foreach (var role in ThriftLoop.ViewModels.Admin.UserManagementViewModel.RoleFilters.Where(r => r != "All"))
                    {
                    <option value="@role" selected="@(Model.RoleFilter == role)">@role</option>
                }
            </select>
            <button type="submit" class="btn-filter">Filter</button>
            <a asp-action="Users" class="btn-clear">Clear</a>
        </div>
    </form>

    <!-- Users Table -->
    <div class="table-container">
        <table class="admin-table">
            <thead>
                <tr>
                    <th>ID</th>
                    <th>Email</th>
                    <th>Role</th>
                    <th>Status</th>
                    <th>Joined</th>
                    <th>Actions</th>
                </tr>
            </thead>
            <tbody>
                @foreach (var user in Model.Users)
                {
                    <tr>
                        <td>@user.Id</td>
                        <td>@user.Email</td>
                        <td>
                            <form method="post" asp-action="UpdateUserRole" class="inline-form">
                                @Html.AntiForgeryToken()
                                <input type="hidden" name="userId" value="@user.Id" />
                                <select name="newRole" class="role-select" onchange="this.form.submit()">
                                    @foreach (UserRole role in Enum.GetValues(typeof(UserRole)))
                                    {
                                        if (role == UserRole.Rider) continue;
                                        <option value="@role" selected="@(user.Role == role)">@role</option>
                                    }
                                </select>
                            </form>
                        </td>
                        <td>
                            <span class="status-badge @(user.IsDisabled ? "status-disabled" : "status-active")">
                                @(user.IsDisabled ? "Disabled" : "Active")
                            </span>
                        </td>
                        <td>@user.CreatedAt.ToString("yyyy-MM-dd")</td>
                        <td>
                            <form method="post" asp-action="ToggleUserStatus" class="inline-form">
                                @Html.AntiForgeryToken()
                                <input type="hidden" name="userId" value="@user.Id" />
                                <input type="hidden" name="isDisabled" value="@(!user.IsDisabled)" />
                                <button type="submit" class="action-btn @(user.IsDisabled ? "btn-enable" : "btn-disable")"
                                        onclick="return confirm('@(user.IsDisabled ? "Enable" : "Disable") user @user.Email?')">
                                    @(user.IsDisabled ? "Enable" : "Disable")
                                </button>
                            </form>
                        </td>
                    </tr>
                }
            </tbody>
        </table>
    </div>

    <!-- Pagination -->
    @if (Model.TotalPages > 1)
    {
        <div class="pagination">
            @if (Model.HasPreviousPage)
            {
                <a asp-action="Users" asp-route-page="@(Model.CurrentPage - 1)" asp-route-search="@Model.SearchTerm" asp-route-role="@Model.RoleFilter" class="page-link">← Previous</a>
            }
            <span class="page-current">Page @Model.CurrentPage of @Model.TotalPages</span>
            @if (Model.HasNextPage)
            {
                <a asp-action="Users" asp-route-page="@(Model.CurrentPage + 1)" asp-route-search="@Model.SearchTerm" asp-route-role="@Model.RoleFilter" class="page-link">Next →</a>
            }
        </div>
    }
</div>

                    <th>Actions</th>
                </tr>

                        <td>@wd.User?.Email</td>

                        <td>@(wd.Method == WithdrawalMethod.BankTransfer ? "Bank Transfer" : "Pickup")</td>
                        <td>@(wd.Reference ?? "—")</td>
                        <td>@wd.RequestedAt.ToString("yyyy-MM-dd")</td>
                        <td>
                            <span class="status-badge status-@wd.Status.ToString().ToLower()">@wd.Status</span>
                        </td>
                        <td>
                            @if (wd.Status == WithdrawalStatus.Requested)
                            {
                                <form method="post" asp-action="ProcessWithdrawal" class="inline-form">
                                    @Html.AntiForgeryToken()
                                    <input type="hidden" name="withdrawalId" value="@wd.Id" />
                                    <button type="submit" class="action-btn btn-process">Mark Processed</button>
                                </form>
                            }
                            else if (wd.Status == WithdrawalStatus.Processed)
                            {
                                <form method="post" asp-action="CompleteWithdrawal" class="inline-form">
                                    @Html.AntiForgeryToken()
                                    <input type="hidden" name="withdrawalId" value="@wd.Id" />
                                    <button type="submit" class="action-btn btn-complete">Mark Completed</button>
                                </form>
                            }
                            else
                            {
                                <span class="action-disabled">—</span>
                            }
                        </td>
                    </tr>
                }
            </tbody>
        </table>
    </div>

    @if (!Model.Any())
    {
        <div class="empty-state">
            <p>No withdrawals found.</p>
        </div>
    }
</div>

<!DOCTYPE html>
<html lang="en">
<head>
    <meta charset="utf-8" />
    <meta name="viewport" content="width=device-width, initial-scale=1.0" />
    <title>@ViewData["Title"] - ThriftLoop</title>
    <link rel="preconnect" href="https://fonts.googleapis.com">
    <link rel="preconnect" href="https://fonts.gstatic.com" crossorigin>

    <link rel="stylesheet" href="~/css/Auth.css" asp-append-version="true" />

<body>
    <div class="auth-shell">

        <aside class="auth-panel auth-panel--brand">
            <div class="brand-wordmark">ThriftLoop</div>
            <p class="brand-tagline">Second-hand style.<br>First-class finds.</p>
            <div class="brand-decoration" aria-hidden="true">
                <span class="deco-ring deco-ring--lg"></span>

            <div class="form-card">

                <header class="form-card__header">
                    <h1 class="form-card__title">Welcome back</h1>
                    <p class="form-card__subtitle">Sign in to continue to ThriftLoop</p>
                </header>

                @* Google error (e.g. OAuth cancelled) *@
                @if (TempData["ExternalAuthError"] is string extError)
                {
                    <div class="alert alert--error" role="alert">
                        <svg viewBox="0 0 20 20" fill="currentColor" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M10 18a8 8 0 100-16 8 8 0 000 16zm-.75-4.75a.75.75 0 001.5 0v-4.5a.75.75 0 00-1.5 0v4.5zm.75-7a.75.75 0 110 1.5.75.75 0 010-1.5z" clip-rule="evenodd" /></svg>
                        <span>@extError</span>
                    </div>
                }

                @* Successful password reset redirect *@
                @if (TempData["ResetSuccess"] is string resetMsg)
                {
                    <div class="alert alert--success" role="alert">
                        <svg viewBox="0 0 20 20" fill="currentColor" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M10 18a8 8 0 100-16 8 8 0 000 16zm3.857-9.809a.75.75 0 00-1.214-.882l-3.483 4.79-1.88-1.88a.75.75 0 10-1.06 1.061l2.5 2.5a.75.75 0 001.137-.089l4-5.5z" clip-rule="evenodd" /></svg>
                        <span>@resetMsg</span>
                    </div>
                }

                @* Invalid reset link redirect *@
                @if (TempData["ResetError"] is string resetErr)
                {
                    <div class="alert alert--error" role="alert">
                        <svg viewBox="0 0 20 20" fill="currentColor" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M10 18a8 8 0 100-16 8 8 0 000 16zm-.75-4.75a.75.75 0 001.5 0v-4.5a.75.75 0 00-1.5 0v4.5zm.75-7a.75.75 0 110 1.5.75.75 0 010-1.5z" clip-rule="evenodd" /></svg>
                        <span>@resetErr</span>
                    </div>
                }

                @if (!ViewData.ModelState.IsValid)
                {
                    <div class="alert alert--error" role="alert">
                        <svg viewBox="0 0 20 20" fill="currentColor" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M10 18a8 8 0 100-16 8 8 0 000 16zm-.75-4.75a.75.75 0 001.5 0v-4.5a.75.75 0 00-1.5 0v4.5zm.75-7a.75.75 0 110 1.5.75.75 0 010-1.5z" clip-rule="evenodd" /></svg>
                        <div asp-validation-summary="ModelOnly"></div>
                    </div>
                }

                <a asp-action="GoogleLogin" asp-controller="Auth"
                   asp-route-returnUrl="@returnUrl"
                   class="btn btn--google">
                    <svg viewBox="0 0 24 24" aria-hidden="true">
                        <path fill="#4285F4" d="M22.56 12.25c0-.78-.07-1.53-.2-2.25H12v4.26h5.92c-.26 1.37-1.04 2.53-2.21 3.31v2.77h3.57c2.08-1.92 3.28-4.74 3.28-8.09z" />
                        <path fill="#34A853" d="M12 23c2.97 0 5.46-.98 7.28-2.66l-3.57-2.77c-.98.66-2.23 1.06-3.71 1.06-2.86 0-5.29-1.93-6.16-4.53H2.18v2.84C3.99 20.53 7.7 23 12 23z" />
                        <path fill="#FBBC05" d="M5.84 14.09c-.22-.66-.35-1.36-.35-2.09s.13-1.43.35-2.09V7.07H2.18C1.43 8.55 1 10.22 1 12s.43 3.45 1.18 4.93l3.66-2.84z" />
                        <path fill="#EA4335" d="M12 5.38c1.62 0 3.06.56 4.21 1.64l3.15-3.15C17.45 2.09 14.97 1 12 1 7.7 1 3.99 3.47 2.18 7.07l3.66 2.84c.87-2.6 3.3-4.53 6.16-4.53z" />
                    </svg>
                    Continue with Google
                </a>

                <div class="auth-divider">
                    <span>or sign in with email</span>
                </div>

                <form asp-action="Login" asp-controller="Auth" asp-route-returnUrl="@returnUrl"
                      method="post" novalidate class="auth-form">
                    @Html.AntiForgeryToken()

                    <div class="field">
                        <label asp-for="Email" class="field__label"></label>
                        <input asp-for="Email"
                               class="field__input"
                               type="email"
                               autocomplete="email"
                               placeholder="you@example.com"
                               spellcheck="false" />
                        <span asp-validation-for="Email" class="field__error"></span>
                    </div>

                                   placeholder="••••••••" />

                                <svg viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2"><path d="M1 12s4-8 11-8 11 8 11 8-4 8-11 8-11-8-11-8z" /><circle cx="12" cy="12" r="3" /></svg>
                            </button>
                        </div>
                        <span asp-validation-for="Password" class="field__error"></span>
                    </div>

                        <label class="checkbox-label">
                            <input asp-for="RememberMe" type="checkbox" class="checkbox-input" />

                        </label>
                    </div>

                    </button>
                </form>

                <footer class="form-card__footer">

                    </p>

    <script src="https://cdnjs.cloudflare.com/ajax/libs/jquery-validate/1.19.5/jquery.validate.min.js"></script>

    <script>
        function togglePassword(inputId) {
        const input = document.getElementById(inputId);
        input.type = input.type === 'password' ? 'text' : 'password';
        }

        document.getElementById('passwordInput').addEventListener('input', function () {
        const val  = this.value;
        const fill = document.getElementById('strengthFill');
        let strength = 0;
        if (val.length >= 8)          strength++;
        if (/[A-Z]/.test(val))        strength++;
        if (/[0-9]/.test(val))        strength++;
        if (/[^A-Za-z0-9]/.test(val)) strength++;

        const pct = (strength / 4) * 100;
        fill.style.width = pct + '%';
        fill.className   = 'strength-bar__fill';
        if (strength <= 1)      fill.classList.add('strength-bar__fill--weak');
        else if (strength <= 2) fill.classList.add('strength-bar__fill--fair');
        else if (strength <= 3) fill.classList.add('strength-bar__fill--good');
        else                    fill.classList.add('strength-bar__fill--strong');
        });
    </script>
</body>
</html>

--- Views/Auth/RiderApproval.cshtml ---

@{
    ViewData["Title"] = "Rider Application Status";
    Layout = null;
    var isApproved = (bool)(ViewBag.IsApproved ?? false);
    var rejectionReason = ViewBag.RejectionReason as string;
    // Read timestamps provided by controller
    DateTime? rejectedAt = ViewBag.RejectedAt as DateTime?;
    DateTime? resubmittedAt = ViewBag.ResubmittedAt as DateTime?;

    // Use controller-provided CanEdit when available; otherwise fall back to legacy logic
    var canEdit = (bool)(ViewBag.CanEdit ?? (!isApproved && !string.IsNullOrEmpty(rejectionReason) && (resubmittedAt == null || (rejectedAt != null && resubmittedAt <= rejectedAt))));
}

                    </div>

    <script src="https://cdnjs.cloudflare.com/ajax/libs/jquery/3.6.0/jquery.min.js"></script>
    <script src="https://cdnjs.cloudflare.com/ajax/libs/jquery-validate/1.19.5/jquery.validate.min.js"></script>

    <script>
        function togglePassword(inputId) {
        const input = document.getElementById(inputId);
        input.type = input.type === 'password' ? 'text' : 'password';
        }

        document.getElementById('passwordInput').addEventListener('input', function() {
        const val = this.value;
        const fill = document.getElementById('strengthFill');
        let strength = 0;
        if (val.length >= 8) strength++;
        if (/[A-Z]/.test(val)) strength++;
        if (/[0-9]/.test(val)) strength++;
        if (/[^A-Za-z0-9]/.test(val)) strength++;
        const pct = (strength / 4) * 100;
        fill.style.width = pct + '%';
        fill.className = 'strength-bar__fill';
        if (strength <= 1) fill.classList.add('strength-bar__fill--weak');
        else if (strength <= 2) fill.classList.add('strength-bar__fill--fair');
        else if (strength <= 3) fill.classList.add('strength-bar__fill--good');
        else fill.classList.add('strength-bar__fill--strong');
        });

        function previewLicense(input) {
        const preview = document.getElementById('licensePreview');
        const body = document.getElementById('licenseUploadBody');
        if (input.files && input.files[0]) {
        if (input.files[0].size > 5 * 1024 * 1024) {
        alert('File exceeds 5 MB. Please choose a smaller image.');
        input.value = '';
        return;
        }
        const reader = new FileReader();
        reader.onload = function(e) {
        preview.src = e.target.result;
        preview.style.display = 'block';
        body.style.display = 'none';
        };
        reader.readAsDataURL(input.files[0]);
        }
        }

        document.querySelector('[name="LicensePlate"]')
        ?.addEventListener('blur', function() { this.value = this.value.toUpperCase(); });
    </script>
</body>
</html>

        </main>
    </div>

    <script>
            (function() {
                var grid = document.getElementById('itemGrid');
                var filterEmpty = document.getElementById('filterEmpty');
                var visibleCount = document.getElementById('visibleCount');

                if (!grid && !filterEmpty) return;

                if (grid) {
                    var cards = Array.prototype.slice.call(grid.querySelectorAll('.fy-card'));

                    // Multi-image hover cycling
                    cards.forEach(function(card) {
                        var wrap = card.querySelector('.fy-card__img-wrap');
                        var img = card.querySelector('.fy-card__img');
                        var dotsEl = card.querySelector('.fy-card__dots');

                        if (!wrap || !img) return;

                        var raw = wrap.getAttribute('data-images');
                        var images = [];
                        try { images = JSON.parse(raw); } catch (e) { }
                        if (images.length < 2) return;

                        var dots = dotsEl ? Array.prototype.slice.call(dotsEl.querySelectorAll('.fy-card__dot')) : [];
                        var current = 0;
                        var timer = null;

                        function goTo(idx) {
                            img.classList.add('fy-img--fading');
                            setTimeout(function() {
                                img.src = images[idx];
                                img.classList.remove('fy-img--fading');
                            }, 220);
                            dots.forEach(function(d, i) {
                                d.classList.toggle('fy-card__dot--active', i === idx);
                            });
                            current = idx;
                        }

                        card.addEventListener('mouseenter', function() {
                            if (timer) return;
                            timer = setInterval(function() { goTo((current + 1) % images.length); }, 900);
                        });
                        card.addEventListener('mouseleave', function() {
                            if (timer) { clearInterval(timer); timer = null; }
                            if (current !== 0) goTo(0);
                        });
                    });

                    // Filter callback
                    window.applyFiltersCallback = function(state) {
                        var query = state.search.toLowerCase();
                        var minVal = state.priceMin;
                        var maxVal = state.priceMax;
                        var activeCats = state.categories;
                        var activeConds = state.conditions;

                        var shown = 0;

                        cards.forEach(function(card) {
                            var cat = card.dataset.category;
                            var cond = card.dataset.condition;
                            var price = parseFloat(card.dataset.price);
                            var title = card.dataset.title || '';
                            var desc = card.dataset.desc || '';

                            var catOk = activeCats.length === 0 || activeCats.indexOf(cat) !== -1;
                            var condOk = activeConds.length === 0 || activeConds.indexOf(cond) !== -1;
                            var priceOk = price >= minVal && price <= maxVal;
                            var textOk = !query || title.indexOf(query) !== -1 || desc.indexOf(query) !== -1;

                            var visible = catOk && condOk && priceOk && textOk;
                            card.classList.toggle('fy-card--hidden', !visible);
                            if (visible) shown++;
                        });

                        if (visibleCount) visibleCount.textContent = shown;
                        if (filterEmpty) filterEmpty.classList.toggle('fy-empty--hidden', shown > 0);
                    };
                }

                // Reset button inside empty state
                var resetBtn2 = document.getElementById('resetFilters2');
                if (resetBtn2) {
                    resetBtn2.addEventListener('click', function() {
                        if (window.resetFiltersFromPartial) {
                            window.resetFiltersFromPartial();
                        }
                    });
                }
            }());
    </script>
</body>
</html>

                                Post Listing
                            </button>
                            <a asp-action="Index" asp-controller="Home" class="btn btn--ghost">Cancel</a>
                        </div>

                    </div>
                </div>
            </form>
        </div>
    </div>

    <script src="https://cdnjs.cloudflare.com/ajax/libs/jquery/3.6.0/jquery.min.js"></script>
    <script src="https://cdnjs.cloudflare.com/ajax/libs/jquery-validate/1.19.5/jquery.validate.min.js"></script>
    <script src="https://cdnjs.cloudflare.com/ajax/libs/jquery-validation-unobtrusive/3.2.12/jquery.validate.unobtrusive.min.js"></script>
    <script>
        (function () {
            'use strict';

            var MAX_PHOTOS = 5;
            var fileList   = new DataTransfer(); // virtual file list maintained by JS

            // ── DOM refs ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
            var addZone    = document.getElementById('photoAddZone');
            var photosInput = document.getElementById('photosInput');
            var thumbsEl   = document.getElementById('photoThumbs');
            var photoErr   = document.getElementById('photoErr');
            var form       = document.getElementById('createForm');
            var submitBtn  = document.getElementById('submitBtn');
            var banner     = document.getElementById('validationBanner');
            var bannerText = document.getElementById('validationBannerText');

            // ── Photo: add zone click / drag ──────────────────────────────────────
            addZone.addEventListener('click', function () { photosInput.click(); });

            addZone.addEventListener('dragover', function (e) {
                e.preventDefault();
                addZone.classList.add('photo-add-zone--drag');
            });
            addZone.addEventListener('dragleave', function () {
                addZone.classList.remove('photo-add-zone--drag');
            });
            addZone.addEventListener('drop', function (e) {
                e.preventDefault();
                addZone.classList.remove('photo-add-zone--drag');
                addFiles(Array.from(e.dataTransfer.files));
            });

            photosInput.addEventListener('change', function () {
                var selectedFiles = Array.from(photosInput.files); // capture BEFORE clearing
                photosInput.value = '';                            // reset native picker
                addFiles(selectedFiles);                           // syncInput runs last → files stay
            });

            function addFiles(files) {
                var errors = [];
                for (var i = 0; i < files.length; i++) {
                    if (fileList.files.length >= MAX_PHOTOS) break;
                    var f = files[i];
                    if (!['image/jpeg','image/png','image/webp'].includes(f.type)) {
                        errors.push('Only JPEG, PNG, or WebP images are accepted.');
                        continue;
                    }
                    if (f.size > 5 * 1024 * 1024) {
                        errors.push(f.name + ' exceeds 5 MB.');
                        continue;
                    }
                    fileList.items.add(f);
                }
                if (errors.length) photoErr.textContent = errors[0];
                syncInput();
                renderThumbs();
            }

            function removeFile(idx) {
                var newDt = new DataTransfer();
                Array.from(fileList.files).forEach(function (f, i) {
                    if (i !== idx) newDt.items.add(f);
                });
                fileList = newDt;
                syncInput();
                renderThumbs();
            }

            function syncInput() {
                photosInput.files = fileList.files;
            }

            function renderThumbs() {
                thumbsEl.innerHTML = '';
                var files = Array.from(fileList.files);
                files.forEach(function (file, i) {
                    var div = document.createElement('div');
                    div.className = 'photo-thumb';

                    var img = document.createElement('img');
                    img.alt = 'Photo ' + (i + 1);
                    var reader = new FileReader();
                    reader.onload = function (e) { img.src = e.target.result; };
                    reader.readAsDataURL(file);
                    div.appendChild(img);

                    if (i === 0) {
                        var badge = document.createElement('span');
                        badge.className = 'photo-thumb__badge';
                        badge.textContent = 'Cover';
                        div.appendChild(badge);
                    }

                    var rm = document.createElement('button');
                    rm.type = 'button';
                    rm.className = 'photo-thumb__remove';
                    rm.innerHTML = '×';
                    rm.setAttribute('aria-label', 'Remove photo');
                    (function (idx) {
                        rm.addEventListener('click', function () { removeFile(idx); });
                    }(i));
                    div.appendChild(rm);

                    thumbsEl.appendChild(div);
                });

                // Show/hide add zone
                if (files.length >= MAX_PHOTOS) {
                    addZone.classList.add('photo-add-zone--hidden');
                } else {
                    addZone.classList.remove('photo-add-zone--hidden');
                }

                // Clear photo error when thumbs are present
                if (files.length > 0) photoErr.textContent = '';
            }

            // ── Character counters ────────────────────────────────────────────────
            function initCounter(inputId, counterId, max) {
                var input   = document.getElementById(inputId);
                var counter = document.getElementById(counterId);
                if (!input || !counter) return;
                var update = function () {
                    var len = input.value.length;
                    counter.textContent = len + '/' + max;
                    counter.classList.toggle('create-field__counter--warn', len > max * 0.9);
                };
                input.addEventListener('input', update);
                update();
            }
            initCounter('titleInput', 'titleCounter', 100);
            initCounter('descInput',  'descCounter',  1000);

            // ── Required chips (category, condition) ──────────────────────────────
            function initChips(containerId) {
                var container = document.getElementById(containerId);
                if (!container) return;
                container.addEventListener('click', function (e) {
                    var btn = e.target.closest('[data-value]');
                    if (!btn) return;
                    var select = document.getElementById(btn.dataset.target);
                    if (!select) return;
                    container.querySelectorAll('[data-value]').forEach(function (b) {
                        b.classList.remove('create-chip--active','create-condition__pill--active');
                    });
                    btn.classList.add(containerId === 'categoryChips' ? 'create-chip--active' : 'create-condition__pill--active');
                    select.value = btn.dataset.value;
                    // Clear the error for this field
                    var errId = containerId === 'categoryChips' ? 'categoryErr' : 'conditionErr';
                    var errEl = document.getElementById(errId);
                    if (errEl) errEl.textContent = '';
                    container.classList.remove('chips-error');
                });
            }
            initChips('categoryChips');
            initChips('conditionPills');

            // ── Optional chips (size) — second click deselects ────────────────────
            (function () {
                var container = document.getElementById('sizeChips');
                var select    = document.getElementById('sizeSelect');
                if (!container || !select) return;
                container.addEventListener('click', function (e) {
                    var btn = e.target.closest('[data-value]');
                    if (!btn) return;
                    var already = btn.classList.contains('create-chip--active');
                    container.querySelectorAll('[data-value]').forEach(function (b) {
                        b.classList.remove('create-chip--active');
                    });
                    if (already) { select.value = ''; }
                    else { btn.classList.add('create-chip--active'); select.value = btn.dataset.value; }
                });
            }());

            // ── Duration chips ────────────────────────────────────────────────────
            (function () {
                var container = document.getElementById('durationChips');
                var select    = document.getElementById('stealDurationSelect');
                if (!container || !select) return;
                container.addEventListener('click', function (e) {
                    var btn = e.target.closest('[data-value]');
                    if (!btn) return;
                    container.querySelectorAll('[data-value]').forEach(function (b) {
                        b.classList.remove('create-chip--active');
                    });
                    btn.classList.add('create-chip--active');
                    select.value = btn.dataset.value;
                    var errEl = document.getElementById('durationErr');
                    if (errEl) errEl.textContent = '';
                    container.classList.remove('chips-error');
                });
            }());

            // ── Stealable toggle ──────────────────────────────────────────────────
            (function () {
                var checkbox = document.getElementById('IsStealable');
                var panel    = document.getElementById('stealDurationPanel');
                var durSel   = document.getElementById('stealDurationSelect');
                if (!checkbox || !panel) return;
                function sync() {
                    if (checkbox.checked) {
                        panel.removeAttribute('hidden');
                    } else {
                        panel.setAttribute('hidden', '');
                        if (durSel) { durSel.value = ''; }
                        document.querySelectorAll('#durationChips [data-value]').forEach(function (b) {
                            b.classList.remove('create-chip--active');
                        });
                    }
                }
                checkbox.addEventListener('change', sync);
                sync();
            }());

            // ── Auto-clear input errors on change ────────────────────────────────
            function bindClearError(inputId, errId, wrapId) {
                var el = document.getElementById(inputId);
                if (!el) return;
                el.addEventListener('input', function () {
                    el.classList.remove('input-error');
                    if (wrapId) document.getElementById(wrapId) && document.getElementById(wrapId).classList.remove('input-error');
                    var errEl = document.getElementById(errId);
                    if (errEl) errEl.textContent = '';
                    if (banner.style.display !== 'none') {
                        // Re-check if any errors remain
                        var anyErr = document.querySelectorAll('.input-error, .chips-error, .field__error:not(:empty)').length;
                        if (!anyErr) banner.style.display = 'none';
                    }
                });
            }
            bindClearError('titleInput', 'titleErr');
            bindClearError('descInput',  'descErr');
            bindClearError('priceInput', 'priceErr', 'priceWrap');

            // ── Client-side form validation ───────────────────────────────────────
            function showErr(errId, msg) {
                var el = document.getElementById(errId);
                if (el) el.textContent = msg;
            }
            function markInputErr(inputId, wrapId) {
                var el = document.getElementById(inputId);
                if (el) el.classList.add('input-error');
                if (wrapId) { var w = document.getElementById(wrapId); if (w) w.classList.add('input-error'); }
                return el;
            }
            function markChipsErr(containerId) {
                var el = document.getElementById(containerId);
                if (el) el.classList.add('chips-error');
                return el;
            }

            function validate() {
                var firstErrEl = null;
                var ok = true;

                // Clear previous
                ['titleErr','descErr','priceErr','categoryErr','conditionErr','durationErr','photoErr'].forEach(function (id) {
                    var el = document.getElementById(id); if (el) el.textContent = '';
                });
                document.querySelectorAll('.input-error').forEach(function (el) { el.classList.remove('input-error'); });
                document.querySelectorAll('.chips-error').forEach(function (el) { el.classList.remove('chips-error'); });

                // Title
                var titleEl = document.getElementById('titleInput');
                var titleLen = titleEl ? titleEl.value.trim().length : 0;
                if (titleLen < 3 || titleLen > 100) {
                    showErr('titleErr', 'Title must be between 3 and 100 characters.');
                    firstErrEl = firstErrEl || markInputErr('titleInput');
                    ok = false;
                }

                // Description
                var descEl = document.getElementById('descInput');
                var descLen = descEl ? descEl.value.trim().length : 0;
                if (descLen < 10 || descLen > 1000) {
                    showErr('descErr', 'Description must be between 10 and 1 000 characters.');
                    firstErrEl = firstErrEl || markInputErr('descInput');
                    ok = false;
                }

                // Price
                var priceEl = document.getElementById('priceInput');
                var priceVal = priceEl ? parseFloat(priceEl.value) : NaN;
                if (!priceEl || !priceEl.value || isNaN(priceVal) || priceVal < 0.01 || priceVal > 99999.99) {
                    showErr('priceErr', 'Price must be between ₱0.01 and ₱99,999.99.');
                    firstErrEl = firstErrEl || markInputErr('priceInput', 'priceWrap');
                    ok = false;
                }

                // Category
                var catSel = document.getElementById('categorySelect');
                if (!catSel || !catSel.value) {
                    showErr('categoryErr', 'Please select a category.');
                    firstErrEl = firstErrEl || markChipsErr('categoryChips');
                    ok = false;
                }

                // Condition
                var condSel = document.getElementById('conditionSelect');
                if (!condSel || !condSel.value) {
                    showErr('conditionErr', 'Please select a condition.');
                    firstErrEl = firstErrEl || markChipsErr('conditionPills');
                    ok = false;
                }

                // Steal duration
                var stealChk = document.getElementById('IsStealable');
                if (stealChk && stealChk.checked) {
                    var durSel = document.getElementById('stealDurationSelect');
                    if (!durSel || !durSel.value) {
                        showErr('durationErr', 'Please select a Steal window duration.');
                        firstErrEl = firstErrEl || markChipsErr('durationChips');
                        ok = false;
                    }
                }

                if (!ok) {
                    banner.style.display = 'flex';
                    if (firstErrEl) firstErrEl.scrollIntoView({ behavior: 'smooth', block: 'center' });
                } else {
                    banner.style.display = 'none';
                }

                return ok;
            }

            // ── Submit handler ────────────────────────────────────────────────────
            form.addEventListener('submit', function (e) {
                e.preventDefault(); // Always prevent — let our validate() decide
                if (!validate()) return;
                submitBtn.disabled = true;
                submitBtn.innerHTML = '<svg class="spin" viewBox="0 0 20 20" fill="currentColor" width="16" height="16"><path d="M10 3a7 7 0 100 14A7 7 0 0010 3z" opacity=".25"/></svg> Posting…';
                form.submit(); // Programmatic submit bypasses event listeners
            });

            // ── Auto-dismiss toast ────────────────────────────────────────────────
            var toast = document.querySelector('.create-toast');
            if (toast) {
                setTimeout(function () {
                    toast.style.opacity = '0';
                    setTimeout(function () { toast.remove(); }, 400);
                }, 4000);
            }

        }());
    </script>
</body>
</html>

--- Views/Items/Details.cshtml ---
@model ThriftLoop.Models.Item
@using ThriftLoop.Models
@using ThriftLoop.Enums
@{
    ViewData["Title"] = Model.Title;
    Layout = null;

    bool isOwner = (bool)(ViewBag.IsOwner ?? false);
    bool isAnonymous = (bool)(ViewBag.IsAnonymous ?? true);
    bool isCurrentWinner = (bool)(ViewBag.IsCurrentWinner ?? false);
    bool isOriginalGetter = (bool)(ViewBag.IsOriginalGetter ?? false);

    bool isStealable = Model.ListingType == ListingType.Stealable;
    bool stealWindowOpen = isStealable
                           && Model.Status == ItemStatus.Reserved
                           && Model.StealEndsAt.HasValue
                           && DateTime.UtcNow <= Model.StealEndsAt.Value;

    string sellerDisplay = Model.User is not null
        ? Model.User.Email.Split('@')[0]
        : "Unknown seller";

    string condClass = Model.Condition switch
    {
        "New" => "detail-condition--new",
        "Like New" => "detail-condition--like-new",
        "Good" => "detail-condition--good",
        "Fair" => "detail-condition--fair",
        _ => "detail-condition--poor"
    };

    string priceLabel = isStealable ? "Starting price" : "Fixed price";
    if (isStealable && Model.Status == ItemStatus.Reserved)
        priceLabel = "Current price";
    if (isStealable && Model.Status == ItemStatus.StolenPendingCheckout)
        priceLabel = "Stolen price";

    bool hasImages = Model.ImageUrls.Count > 0;
}

<!DOCTYPE html>
<html lang="en">

    <meta charset="utf-8" />

    <link rel="stylesheet" href="~/css/Navbar.css" asp-append-version="true" />
</head>
<body>
    @await Html.PartialAsync("_Navbar")

    <div class="detail-shell">

        @* ── Back navigation ────────────────────────────────────────────────────── *@

                </svg>
                Back to listings
            </a>
        </nav>

        @* ── Two-column layout ──────────────────────────────────────────────────── *@
        <div class="detail-grid">

            @* ════════════════════════════════
               LEFT — Image Gallery
               ════════════════════════════════ *@
            <aside class="detail-img-col">

                <div class="detail-gallery">

                    @* ── Main image display ── *@
                    <div class="detail-img-frame" id="galleryMain">
                        @if (hasImages)
                        {
                            <img src="@Model.ImageUrls[0]"
                                 id="mainGalleryImg"
                                 alt="Photo of @Model.Title"
                                 class="detail-img"
                                 loading="eager" />

                            @if (Model.ImageUrls.Count > 1)
                            {
                                <button type="button" class="gallery-arrow gallery-arrow--prev" id="galleryPrev" aria-label="Previous photo">
                                    <svg viewBox="0 0 20 20" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" width="18" height="18">
                                        <path d="M12.5 5L7.5 10L12.5 15" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" />
                                    </svg>
                                </button>
                                <button type="button" class="gallery-arrow gallery-arrow--next" id="galleryNext" aria-label="Next photo">
                                    <svg viewBox="0 0 20 20" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" width="18" height="18">
                                        <path d="M7.5 5L12.5 10L7.5 15" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" />
                                    </svg>
                                </button>
                                <span class="gallery-counter" id="galleryCounter">
                                    1 / @Model.ImageUrls.Count
                                </span>
                            }
                        }
                        else
                        {
                            <div class="detail-img detail-img--placeholder" aria-hidden="true">
                                <svg viewBox="0 0 64 64" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="1.4">
                                    <rect x="6" y="10" width="52" height="44" rx="6" />
                                    <circle cx="22" cy="26" r="6" />
                                    <path d="M6 46l16-14 10 10 8-7 18 15" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" />
                                </svg>
                                <span>No photo</span>
                            </div>
                        }

                        @if (isStealable)
                        {
                            <span class="detail-stealable-badge" aria-label="Stealable listing">
                                <svg viewBox="0 0 16 16" fill="currentColor" width="12" height="12" aria-hidden="true">
                                    <path d="M8.75 3.75a.75.75 0 00-1.5 0v2.5h-2.5a.75.75 0 000 1.5h2.5v2.5a.75.75 0 001.5 0v-2.5h2.5a.75.75 0 000-1.5h-2.5v-2.5z" />
                                </svg>
                                Stealable
                            </span>
                        }
                    </div>

                    @if (Model.ImageUrls.Count > 1)
                    {
                        <div class="gallery-thumbs" id="galleryThumbs" role="list">
                            @for (int t = 0; t < Model.ImageUrls.Count; t++)
                            {
                                <button type="button"
                                        class="gallery-thumb @(t == 0 ? "gallery-thumb--active" : "")"
                                        data-index="@t"
                                        data-src="@Model.ImageUrls[t]"
                                        role="listitem"
                                        aria-label="Photo @(t + 1)">
                                    <img src="@Model.ImageUrls[t]" alt="Thumbnail @(t + 1)" loading="lazy" />
                                    @if (t == 0)
                                    {
                                        <span class="gallery-thumb__cover">Cover</span>
                                    }
                                </button>
                            }
                        </div>
                    }

                </div>

                @* Seller card *@
                <div class="detail-seller detail-seller--below-img">
                    <div class="detail-seller__avatar" aria-hidden="true">
                        @sellerDisplay.Substring(0, 1).ToUpper()
                    </div>
                    <div class="detail-seller__info">
                        <p class="detail-seller__label">Listed by</p>
                        <p class="detail-seller__name">@sellerDisplay</p>
                        <p class="detail-seller__since">
                            Member since @(Model.User?.CreatedAt.ToString("MMMM yyyy") ?? "—")
                        </p>
                    </div>
                </div>

            </aside>

            @* ════════════════════════════════
               RIGHT — Details
               ════════════════════════════════ *@
            <section class="detail-info-col">

                <div class="detail-meta-row">
                    <span class="detail-category">@Model.Category</span>
                    <span class="detail-condition @condClass">@Model.Condition</span>
                    @if (!string.IsNullOrEmpty(Model.Size))
                    {
                        <span class="detail-size">@Model.Size</span>
                    }
                    @if (isStealable)
                    {
                        <span class="detail-listing-type-badge">
                            <svg viewBox="0 0 14 14" fill="currentColor" width="10" height="10" aria-hidden="true">
                                <path d="M7 1a6 6 0 100 12A6 6 0 007 1zm.6 8.9H6.4V6.4h1.2v3.5zm0-4.6H6.4V4.1h1.2v1.2z" />
                            </svg>
                            Stealable
                        </span>
                    }
                </div>

                <h1 class="detail-title">@Model.Title</h1>

                <div class="detail-price-block">
                    <span class="detail-price">₱@Model.Price.ToString("N2")</span>

                    {
                        <span class="detail-steal-note">+₱50 if stolen</span>
                    }
                </div>

                @* ── Stealable countdown / status banners ────────────────────────── *@
                @if (isStealable && Model.Status == ItemStatus.Reserved && Model.StealEndsAt.HasValue)
                {
                    if (stealWindowOpen)
                    {
                        <div class="steal-countdown-card" id="stealCountdownCard">
                            <div class="steal-countdown-card__icon" aria-hidden="true">
                                <svg viewBox="0 0 20 20" fill="currentColor" width="18" height="18">
                                    <path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M10 18a8 8 0 100-16 8 8 0 000 16zm.75-13a.75.75 0 00-1.5 0v5c0 .414.336.75.75.75h4a.75.75 0 000-1.5h-3.25V5z" clip-rule="evenodd" />
                                </svg>
                            </div>
                            <div class="steal-countdown-card__body">
                                <p class="steal-countdown-card__label">Steal window closes in</p>

                                   id="stealTimer"

                                </svg>
                            </div>
                            <div class="steal-countdown-card__body">

                                </p>
                            </div>

                                                <path d="M6.28 5.22a.75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06L8.94 10l-3.72 3.72a.75.75 0 101.06 1.06L10 11.06l3.72 3.72a.75.75 0 101.06-1.06L11.06 10l3.72-3.72a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06L10 8.94 6.28 5.22z" />
                                            </svg>

                                                <path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M.458 10C1.732 5.943 5.522 3 10 3s8.268 2.943 9.542 7c-1.274 4.057-5.064 7-9.542 7S1.732 14.057.458 10zM14 10a4 4 0 11-8 0 4 4 0 018 0z" clip-rule="evenodd" />
                                            </svg>

                                        </svg>

                    else if (isStealable && Model.Status == ItemStatus.StolenPendingCheckout)
                    {

                        {

                    @if (TempData["InfoMessage"] is string infoMsg)

                    @* ══ 3e. Stealable — Sold (order confirmed) ══ *@
                    else if (isStealable && Model.Status == ItemStatus.Sold)

                        @* Sold notice is rendered above; no button needed unless still pending *@
                    }
                }

            </section>

        </div>

    </div>

    <script>
        (function () {
            'use strict';

            // ── Gallery (runs only when multi-image elements exist) ───────────────
            (function () {
                var mainImg   = document.getElementById('mainGalleryImg');
                var thumbsEl  = document.getElementById('galleryThumbs');
                var prevBtn   = document.getElementById('galleryPrev');
                var nextBtn   = document.getElementById('galleryNext');
                var counterEl = document.getElementById('galleryCounter');

                // Early-exit is now safely scoped inside a nested IIFE
                // so it does NOT kill the countdown timers below.
                if (!mainImg || !thumbsEl) return;

                var thumbBtns = Array.prototype.slice.call(thumbsEl.querySelectorAll('.gallery-thumb'));
                var total     = thumbBtns.length;
                var current   = 0;

                function goTo(idx) {
                    if (idx === current) return;
                    mainImg.classList.add('gallery-fading');
                    setTimeout(function () {
                        mainImg.src = thumbBtns[idx].dataset.src;
                        mainImg.classList.remove('gallery-fading');
                    }, 200);
                    thumbBtns[current].classList.remove('gallery-thumb--active');
                    thumbBtns[idx].classList.add('gallery-thumb--active');
                    if (counterEl) counterEl.textContent = (idx + 1) + ' / ' + total;
                    current = idx;
                }

                thumbBtns.forEach(function (btn, i) {
                    btn.addEventListener('click', function () { goTo(i); });
                });
                if (prevBtn) prevBtn.addEventListener('click', function () { goTo((current - 1 + total) % total); });
                if (nextBtn) nextBtn.addEventListener('click', function () { goTo((current + 1) % total); });

                document.addEventListener('keydown', function (e) {
                    if (e.key === 'ArrowLeft')  goTo((current - 1 + total) % total);
                    if (e.key === 'ArrowRight') goTo((current + 1) % total);
                });

                var touchStartX = null;
                mainImg.addEventListener('touchstart', function (e) {
                    touchStartX = e.touches[0].clientX;
                }, { passive: true });
                mainImg.addEventListener('touchend', function (e) {
                    if (touchStartX === null) return;
                    var dx = e.changedTouches[0].clientX - touchStartX;
                    touchStartX = null;
                    if (Math.abs(dx) < 40) return;
                    if (dx < 0) goTo((current + 1) % total);
                    else        goTo((current - 1 + total) % total);
                }, { passive: true });
            }());

            // ── Countdown timers — always run regardless of gallery state ─────────
            function startCountdown(el) {
                if (!el) return;
                var endsAt = new Date(el.dataset.endsAt);
                if (endsAt <= new Date()) { el.textContent = '00:00:00'; return; }
                var intervalId = null;
                function tick() {
                    var diffMs = endsAt - new Date();
                    if (diffMs <= 0) {
                        el.textContent = '00:00:00';
                        clearInterval(intervalId);
                        window.location.reload();
                        return;
                    }
                    var s = Math.floor(diffMs / 1000);
                    var h = Math.floor(s / 3600);
                    var m = Math.floor((s % 3600) / 60);
                    el.textContent =
                        String(h).padStart(2, '0') + ':' +
                        String(m).padStart(2, '0') + ':' +
                        String(s % 60).padStart(2, '0');
                }
                tick();
                intervalId = setInterval(tick, 1000);
            }

            // These run unconditionally
            startCountdown(document.getElementById('stealTimer'));
            startCountdown(document.getElementById('finalizeTimer'));

            // ── How-it-works modals ───────────────────────────────────────────────
            var TODAY = new Date().toISOString().slice(0, 10);

            function wasDismissedToday(key) {
                try { return localStorage.getItem(key) === TODAY; } catch(e) { return false; }
            }
            function dismissForToday(key) {
                try { localStorage.setItem(key, TODAY); } catch(e) {}
            }

            function initModal(opts) {
                var overlay    = document.getElementById(opts.overlayId);
                var proceedBtn = document.getElementById(opts.proceedId);
                var dismissChk = document.getElementById(opts.dismissCheckId);
                var triggers   = document.querySelectorAll(opts.triggerSelector);

                if (!overlay || !triggers.length) return;

                function showModal() {
                    overlay.classList.add('hiw-overlay--visible');
                    if (proceedBtn) proceedBtn.focus();
                }
                function hideModal() {
                    overlay.classList.remove('hiw-overlay--visible');
                }
                function proceed() {
                    if (dismissChk && dismissChk.checked) dismissForToday(opts.storageKey);
                    hideModal();
                    opts.onProceed();
                }

                triggers.forEach(function (trigger) {
                    var form = trigger.closest('form');
                    if (form) {
                        form.addEventListener('submit', function (e) {
                            if (wasDismissedToday(opts.storageKey)) return;
                            e.preventDefault();
                            showModal();
                            opts.onProceed = function () { form.submit(); };
                        });
                    }
                });

                if (proceedBtn) proceedBtn.addEventListener('click', proceed);
                overlay.addEventListener('click', function (e) { if (e.target === overlay) hideModal(); });
                document.addEventListener('keydown', function (e) {
                    if (e.key === 'Escape' && overlay.classList.contains('hiw-overlay--visible')) hideModal();
                });
            }

            initModal({
                storageKey:      'thriftloop_hiw_get',
                overlayId:       'hiwGetOverlay',
                proceedId:       'hiwGetProceed',
                dismissCheckId:  'hiwGetDismiss',
                triggerSelector: 'form[action*="GetItem"] button[type="submit"]',
                onProceed:       function () {}
            });

            initModal({
                storageKey:      'thriftloop_hiw_steal',
                overlayId:       'hiwStealOverlay',
                proceedId:       'hiwStealProceed',
                dismissCheckId:  'hiwStealDismiss',
                triggerSelector: 'form[action*="StealItem"] button[type="submit"]',
                onProceed:       function () {}
            });

        }());
    </script>
</body>
</html>

                    @* ── Form Column ──────────────────────────────────────────── *@

                        @* Title *@
                        <div class="create-field">

                                   placeholder="e.g. Vintage Levi's Jacket" maxlength="100" />
                            <span class="field__error" id="titleErr"></span>

                            <textarea asp-for="Description" class="create-field__input create-field__input--textarea"
                                      id="descInput" rows="3" maxlength="1000"
                                      placeholder="Describe the item — colour, fit, any flaws…"></textarea>
