    <script src="https://cdnjs.cloudflare.com/ajax/libs/jquery/3.6.0/jquery.min.js"></script>
    <script src="https://cdnjs.cloudflare.com/ajax/libs/jquery-validate/1.19.5/jquery.validate.min.js"></script>
    <script src="https://cdnjs.cloudflare.com/ajax/libs/jquery-validation-unobtrusive/3.2.12/jquery.validate.unobtrusive.min.js"></script>
    <script>
        (function () {
            'use strict';

            var MAX_PHOTOS = 5;
            var newFileList = new DataTransfer(); // new uploads only

            // ── DOM refs ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
            var form         = document.getElementById('editForm');
            var thumbsEl     = document.getElementById('photoThumbs');
            var addZone      = document.getElementById('photoAddZone');
            var newInput     = document.getElementById('newPhotosInput');
            var photoErr     = document.getElementById('photoErr');
            var submitBtn    = document.getElementById('submitBtn');
            var banner       = document.getElementById('validationBanner');
            var bannerText   = document.getElementById('validationBannerText');

            // ── Helpers: count totals ─────────────────────────────────────────────
            function existingCount() {
                return thumbsEl.querySelectorAll('[data-existing]').length;
            }
            function totalCount() {
                return existingCount() + newFileList.files.length;
            }

            // ── Existing image removal ────────────────────────────────────────────
            // Delegate on thumbsEl so it catches server-rendered buttons.
            thumbsEl.addEventListener('click', function (e) {
                var btn = e.target.closest('[data-existing-url]');
                if (!btn) return;

                var url = btn.getAttribute('data-existing-url');

                // 1. Remove the thumbnail div
                var thumb = btn.closest('[data-existing]');
                if (thumb) thumb.remove();

                // 2. Remove the matching ExistingImageUrls hidden input
                var inputs = form.querySelectorAll('.existing-url-input');
                inputs.forEach(function (inp) {
                    if (inp.value === url) inp.remove();
                });

                // 3. Inject a RemovedImageUrls hidden input so the controller knows to delete the file
                var rmInp = document.createElement('input');
                rmInp.type  = 'hidden';
                rmInp.name  = 'RemovedImageUrls';
                rmInp.value = url;
                form.appendChild(rmInp);

                updateCoverBadge();
                updateAddZone();
            });

            // Reapply "Cover" badge to the new first thumb after any removal
            function updateCoverBadge() {
                thumbsEl.querySelectorAll('.photo-thumb__badge').forEach(function (b) { b.remove(); });
                var firstThumb = thumbsEl.querySelector('.photo-thumb');
                if (firstThumb) {
                    var badge = document.createElement('span');
                    badge.className = 'photo-thumb__badge';
                    badge.textContent = 'Cover';
                    firstThumb.appendChild(badge);
                }
            }

            function updateAddZone() {
                if (totalCount() >= MAX_PHOTOS) {
                    addZone.classList.add('photo-add-zone--hidden');
                } else {
                    addZone.classList.remove('photo-add-zone--hidden');
                }
            }

            // ── New image upload ──────────────────────────────────────────────────
            addZone.addEventListener('click', function () { newInput.click(); });

            addZone.addEventListener('dragover', function (e) {
                e.preventDefault();
                addZone.classList.add('photo-add-zone--drag');
            });
            addZone.addEventListener('dragleave', function () {
                addZone.classList.remove('photo-add-zone--drag');
            });
            addZone.addEventListener('drop', function (e) {
                e.preventDefault();
                addZone.classList.remove('photo-add-zone--drag');
                addNewFiles(Array.from(e.dataTransfer.files));
            });

            newInput.addEventListener('change', function () {
                var selectedFiles = Array.from(newInput.files);
                newInput.value = '';
                addNewFiles(selectedFiles);
            });

            function addNewFiles(files) {
                var errors = [];
                for (var i = 0; i < files.length; i++) {
                    if (totalCount() >= MAX_PHOTOS) break;
                    var f = files[i];
                    if (!['image/jpeg','image/png','image/webp'].includes(f.type)) {
                        errors.push('Only JPEG, PNG, or WebP images are accepted.');
                        continue;
                    }
                    if (f.size > 5 * 1024 * 1024) {
                        errors.push(f.name + ' exceeds 5 MB.');
                        continue;
                    }
                    newFileList.items.add(f);
                    appendNewThumb(f, newFileList.files.length - 1);
                }
                if (errors.length) photoErr.textContent = errors[0];
                newInput.files = newFileList.files;
                updateAddZone();
                updateCoverBadge();
            }

            function appendNewThumb(file, idx) {
                var div = document.createElement('div');
                div.className = 'photo-thumb photo-thumb--new';

                var img = document.createElement('img');
                img.alt = 'New photo';
                var reader = new FileReader();
                reader.onload = function (e) { img.src = e.target.result; };
                reader.readAsDataURL(file);
                div.appendChild(img);

                var badge = document.createElement('span');
                badge.className = 'photo-thumb__badge photo-thumb__badge--new';
                badge.textContent = 'New';
                div.appendChild(badge);

                var rm = document.createElement('button');
                rm.type = 'button';
                rm.className = 'photo-thumb__remove';
                rm.innerHTML = '×';
                rm.setAttribute('aria-label', 'Remove new photo');
                rm.addEventListener('click', function () { removeNewThumb(div, idx); });
                div.appendChild(rm);

                thumbsEl.appendChild(div);
            }

            function removeNewThumb(div, removeIdx) {
                var newDt = new DataTransfer();
                Array.from(newFileList.files).forEach(function (f, i) {
                    if (i !== removeIdx) newDt.items.add(f);
                });
                newFileList = newDt;
                newInput.files = newFileList.files;
                div.remove();
                updateAddZone();
                updateCoverBadge();
            }

            // ── Character counters ────────────────────────────────────────────────
            function initCounter(inputId, counterId, max) {
                var input   = document.getElementById(inputId);
                var counter = document.getElementById(counterId);
                if (!input || !counter) return;
                var update = function () {
                    var len = input.value.length;
                    counter.textContent = len + '/' + max;
                    counter.classList.toggle('create-field__counter--warn', len > max * 0.9);
                };
                input.addEventListener('input', update);
                update();
            }
            initCounter('titleInput', 'titleCounter', 100);
            initCounter('descInput',  'descCounter',  1000);

            // ── Required chips ────────────────────────────────────────────────────
            function initChips(containerId) {
                var container = document.getElementById(containerId);
                if (!container) return;
                container.addEventListener('click', function (e) {
                    var btn = e.target.closest('[data-value]');
                    if (!btn) return;
                    var select = document.getElementById(btn.dataset.target);
                    if (!select) return;
                    container.querySelectorAll('[data-value]').forEach(function (b) {
                        b.classList.remove('create-chip--active','create-condition__pill--active');
                    });
                    btn.classList.add(containerId === 'categoryChips' ? 'create-chip--active' : 'create-condition__pill--active');
                    select.value = btn.dataset.value;
                    var errId = containerId === 'categoryChips' ? 'categoryErr' : 'conditionErr';
                    var errEl = document.getElementById(errId);
                    if (errEl) errEl.textContent = '';
                    container.classList.remove('chips-error');
                });
            }
            initChips('categoryChips');
            initChips('conditionPills');

            // ── Size chips (optional) ─────────────────────────────────────────────
            (function () {
                var container = document.getElementById('sizeChips');
                var select    = document.getElementById('sizeSelect');
                if (!container || !select) return;
                container.addEventListener('click', function (e) {
                    var btn = e.target.closest('[data-value]');
                    if (!btn) return;
                    var already = btn.classList.contains('create-chip--active');
                    container.querySelectorAll('[data-value]').forEach(function (b) { b.classList.remove('create-chip--active'); });
                    if (already) { select.value = ''; }
                    else { btn.classList.add('create-chip--active'); select.value = btn.dataset.value; }
                });
            }());

            // ── Auto-clear input errors ───────────────────────────────────────────
            function bindClearError(inputId, errId, wrapId) {
                var el = document.getElementById(inputId);
                if (!el) return;
                el.addEventListener('input', function () {
                    el.classList.remove('input-error');
                    if (wrapId) { var w = document.getElementById(wrapId); if (w) w.classList.remove('input-error'); }
                    var errEl = document.getElementById(errId);
                    if (errEl) errEl.textContent = '';
                });
            }
            bindClearError('titleInput', 'titleErr');
            bindClearError('descInput',  'descErr');
            bindClearError('priceInput', 'priceErr', 'priceWrap');

            // ── Client-side form validation ───────────────────────────────────────
            function showErr(errId, msg) { var el = document.getElementById(errId); if (el) el.textContent = msg; }
            function markInputErr(inputId, wrapId) {
                var el = document.getElementById(inputId);
                if (el) el.classList.add('input-error');
                if (wrapId) { var w = document.getElementById(wrapId); if (w) w.classList.add('input-error'); }
                return el;
            }
            function markChipsErr(containerId) {
                var el = document.getElementById(containerId);
                if (el) el.classList.add('chips-error');
                return el;
            }

            function validate() {
                var firstErrEl = null;
                var ok = true;

                ['titleErr','descErr','priceErr','categoryErr','conditionErr'].forEach(function (id) {
                    var el = document.getElementById(id); if (el) el.textContent = '';
                });
                document.querySelectorAll('.input-error').forEach(function (el) { el.classList.remove('input-error'); });
                document.querySelectorAll('.chips-error').forEach(function (el) { el.classList.remove('chips-error'); });

                var titleEl = document.getElementById('titleInput');
                var titleLen = titleEl ? titleEl.value.trim().length : 0;
                if (titleLen < 3 || titleLen > 100) {
                    showErr('titleErr', 'Title must be between 3 and 100 characters.');
                    firstErrEl = firstErrEl || markInputErr('titleInput');
                    ok = false;
                }

                var descEl = document.getElementById('descInput');
                var descLen = descEl ? descEl.value.trim().length : 0;
                if (descLen < 10 || descLen > 1000) {
                    showErr('descErr', 'Description must be between 10 and 1 000 characters.');
                    firstErrEl = firstErrEl || markInputErr('descInput');
                    ok = false;
                }

                var priceEl = document.getElementById('priceInput');
                var priceVal = priceEl ? parseFloat(priceEl.value) : NaN;
                if (!priceEl || !priceEl.value || isNaN(priceVal) || priceVal < 0.01 || priceVal > 99999.99) {
                    showErr('priceErr', 'Price must be between ₱0.01 and ₱99,999.99.');
                    firstErrEl = firstErrEl || markInputErr('priceInput', 'priceWrap');
                    ok = false;
                }

                var catSel = document.getElementById('categorySelect');
                if (!catSel || !catSel.value) {
                    showErr('categoryErr', 'Please select a category.');
                    firstErrEl = firstErrEl || markChipsErr('categoryChips');
                    ok = false;
                }

                var condSel = document.getElementById('conditionSelect');
                if (!condSel || !condSel.value) {
                    showErr('conditionErr', 'Please select a condition.');
                    firstErrEl = firstErrEl || markChipsErr('conditionPills');
                    ok = false;
                }

                if (!ok) {
                    banner.style.display = 'flex';
                    if (firstErrEl) firstErrEl.scrollIntoView({ behavior: 'smooth', block: 'center' });
                } else {
                    banner.style.display = 'none';
                }

                return ok;
            }

            // ── Submit handler ────────────────────────────────────────────────────
            form.addEventListener('submit', function (e) {
                e.preventDefault();
                if (!validate()) return;
                submitBtn.disabled = true;
                submitBtn.innerHTML = '<svg class="spin" viewBox="0 0 20 20" fill="currentColor" width="16" height="16"><path d="M10 3a7 7 0 100 14A7 7 0 0010 3z" opacity=".25"/></svg> Saving…';
                form.submit();
            });

        }());
    </script>
</body>
</html>

                                                    <svg viewBox="0 0 20 20" fill="currentColor">

                                                    </svg>
                                                    Delete
                                                </button>
                                            </form>
                                        </div>
                                    </td>

                                </tr>
                            }
                        </tbody>
                    </table>
                </div>
            }
        </div>
    </div>

    <script>
        (function () {
            'use strict';

            // ── Toast auto-dismiss ───────────────────────────────────────────────
            var toast = document.querySelector('.listings-toast');
            if (toast) {
                setTimeout(function () {
                    toast.style.opacity = '0';
                    setTimeout(function () { toast.remove(); }, 400);
                }, 4000);
            }

            // ── Clickable rows ───────────────────────────────────────────────────
            // Navigate to the Details page when the user clicks anywhere on a row
            // that is NOT an interactive element (link, button, or form).
            var rows = document.querySelectorAll('.listings-row--clickable');

            rows.forEach(function (row) {
                row.addEventListener('click', function (e) {
                    // Walk up from the click target — if we hit an interactive element
                    // before reaching the row itself, let the browser handle it normally.
                    if (e.target.closest('a, button, input, form')) return;

                    var href = row.dataset.href;
                    if (href) window.location.href = href;
                });
            });

        }());
    </script>
</body>
</html>

--- Views/Orders/Checkout.cshtml ---

    };

                    </svg>
                    Back to listing
                </a>
            }

        }

                                <div class="co-pay-option__icon">
                                    <svg viewBox="0 0 20 20" fill="currentColor" width="16" height="16">
                                        <path d="M1 4.25a3.733 3.733 0 012-.575h13.5c.43 0 .845.069 1.232.198A2.25 2.25 0 0015.5 3h-11a3 3 0 00-3 3v1.25H1V4.25zM3.75 7A.75.75 0 013 6.25v-.5A2.75 2.75 0 015.75 3h8.5A2.75 2.75 0 0117 5.75v.5a.75.75 0 01-.75.75h-12.5z" />
                                        <path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M1 8.5v6A2.5 2.5 0 003.5 17h13a2.5 2.5 0 002.5-2.5v-6A2.5 2.5 0 0016.5 6h-13A2.5 2.5 0 001 8.5zm14.5 3a1 1 0 100 2 1 1 0 000-2z" clip-rule="evenodd" />
                                    </svg>
                                </div>
                                <div class="co-pay-option__body">
                                    <p class="co-pay-option__name">ThriftLoop Wallet</p>
                                    <p class="co-pay-option__detail">
                                        Balance: <strong>₱@Model.BuyerBalance.ToString("N2")</strong>
                                        @if (!Model.HasSufficientBalance)
                                        {
                                            <span class="co-pay-option__insufficient">
                                                — insufficient
                                                (<a asp-action="AddFunds" asp-controller="Wallet">add funds</a>)
                                            </span>
                                        }
                                        else
                                        {
                                            <text> · funds held in escrow until delivery</text>
                                        }
                                    </p>
                                </div>
                            </label>

                            @* Cash on Delivery option *@
                            <label class="co-pay-option" id="payCodLabel">
                                <input type="radio"
                                       name="__payMethod"
                                       value="Cash"
                                       class="co-pay-radio"
                                       id="payCod"
                                       @(!Model.HasSufficientBalance ? "checked" : "") />
                                <div class="co-pay-option__icon">
                                    <svg viewBox="0 0 20 20" fill="currentColor" width="16" height="16">
                                        <path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M10 18a8 8 0 100-16 8 8 0 000 16zM8.798 7.45c.512-.67 1.135-.95 1.702-.95s1.19.28 1.702.95a.75.75 0 001.192-.91C12.637 5.55 11.596 5 10.5 5s-2.137.55-2.894 1.54A4.501 4.501 0 007 9.5c0 1.079.37 2.077 1 2.879V14a.75.75 0 001.5 0v-1.734c-.35-.588-.5-1.14-.5-1.766 0-.863.275-1.61.798-2.05zM10 14.25a.75.75 0 100 1.5.75.75 0 000-1.5z" clip-rule="evenodd" />
                                    </svg>
                                </div>
                                <div class="co-pay-option__body">
                                    <p class="co-pay-option__name">Cash on Delivery</p>
                                    <p class="co-pay-option__detail">Pay cash when your item arrives</p>
                                </div>
                            </label>

                        </div>
                    </div>

                    @* ── Confirm form: routes to the right action based on order type ── *@
                    @if (Model.IsShopOrder)
                    {
                        <form asp-action="ConfirmShopOrder" asp-controller="Orders"
                              method="post" id="confirmForm">
                            @Html.AntiForgeryToken()
                            <input type="hidden" name="skuId" value="@Model.SkuId" />
                            <input type="hidden" name="quantity" value="@Model.Quantity" />
                            <input type="hidden" name="paymentMethod" id="paymentMethodInput"
                                   value="@(Model.HasSufficientBalance ? "Wallet" : "Cash")" />

                            <button type="submit" class="co-confirm-btn" id="confirmBtn">
                                <svg viewBox="0 0 20 20" fill="currentColor" width="18" height="18" aria-hidden="true">
                                    <path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M16.704 4.153a.75.75 0 01.143 1.052l-8 10.5a.75.75 0 01-1.127.075l-4.5-4.5a.75.75 0 011.06-1.06l3.894 3.893 7.48-9.817a.75.75 0 011.05-.143z" clip-rule="evenodd" />
                                </svg>
                                Confirm Purchase
                            </button>
                        </form>

                        <a asp-action="Details" asp-controller="Shop" asp-route-id="@Model.ItemId"
                           class="co-cancel-link">
                            Cancel and go back
                        </a>
                    }
                    else
                    {
                        <form asp-action="ConfirmOrder" asp-controller="Orders"
                              method="post" id="confirmForm">
                            @Html.AntiForgeryToken()
                            <input type="hidden" name="itemId" value="@Model.ItemId" />
                            <input type="hidden" name="paymentMethod" id="paymentMethodInput"
                                   value="@(Model.HasSufficientBalance ? "Wallet" : "Cash")" />

                            <button type="submit" class="co-confirm-btn" id="confirmBtn">
                                <svg viewBox="0 0 20 20" fill="currentColor" width="18" height="18" aria-hidden="true">
                                    <path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M16.704 4.153a.75.75 0 01.143 1.052l-8 10.5a.75.75 0 01-1.127.075l-4.5-4.5a.75.75 0 011.06-1.06l3.894 3.893 7.48-9.817a.75.75 0 011.05-.143z" clip-rule="evenodd" />
                                </svg>
                                @(Model.WasStolen ? "Confirm Steal Purchase" : "Confirm Purchase")
                            </button>
                        </form>

                        @if (!Model.WasStolen)
                        {
                            <a asp-action="Details" asp-controller="Items" asp-route-id="@Model.ItemId"
                               class="co-cancel-link">
                                Cancel and go back
                            </a>
                        }
                    }

                </div>

            </div>

        </div>

    </div>

    <script>
        (function () {
            'use strict';

            var radios      = document.querySelectorAll('.co-pay-radio');
            var hiddenInput = document.getElementById('paymentMethodInput');
            var form        = document.getElementById('confirmForm');
            var btn         = document.getElementById('confirmBtn');

            // Keep the hidden paymentMethod input in sync with whichever radio is selected
            radios.forEach(function (radio) {
                radio.addEventListener('change', function () {
                    if (hiddenInput) hiddenInput.value = radio.value;
                });
            });

            // Disable button + show spinner on submit to prevent double-confirm
            if (form && btn) {
                form.addEventListener('submit', function () {
                    btn.disabled = true;
                    btn.innerHTML =
                        '<svg class="co-spin" viewBox="0 0 20 20" fill="currentColor" ' +
                        'width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true">' +
                        '<path d="M10 3a7 7 0 100 14A7 7 0 0010 3z" opacity=".3"/>' +
                        '<path d="M10 3a7 7 0 017 7h-1.5A5.5 5.5 0 0010 4.5V3z"/>' +
                        '</svg> Confirming\u2026';
                });
            }

        }());
    </script>
</body>
</html>

                                </h3>
                                <span class="mp-status @statusClass">@statusLabel</span>

                            <p class="mp-row__seller">Seller: @sellerDisplay</p>

                            @* Payment method pill *@
                            <p class="mp-row__pay">
                                <span class="mp-pay-pill mp-pay-pill--@(order.PaymentMethod == PaymentMethod.Wallet ? "wallet" : "cod")">
                                    @if (order.PaymentMethod == PaymentMethod.Wallet)
                                    {
                                        <svg viewBox="0 0 14 14" fill="currentColor" width="10" height="10" aria-hidden="true">
                                            <path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M1 3.5A1.5 1.5 0 012.5 2h9A1.5 1.5 0 0113 3.5v7A1.5 1.5 0 0111.5 12h-9A1.5 1.5 0 011 10.5v-7zm10.5 2.5a.75.75 0 100 1.5.75.75 0 000-1.5z" clip-rule="evenodd" />
                                        </svg>
                                    }
                                    else

                                    @payLabel
                                </span>
                            </p>

                            @* Delivery status message *@

                                <p class="mp-row__delivery" style="font-size: 0.875rem; color: #6b7280; margin: 0.5rem 0;">

                                    @order.OrderDate.ToString("MMMM d, yyyy · h:mm tt") UTC
                                </time>
                            </p>

                            @* Mark Delivered — only visible when delivery is in Delivered state *@
                            @if (canMarkDelivered)
                            {
                                <form asp-action="MarkDelivered"
                                      asp-controller="Orders"
                                      asp-route-orderId="@order.Id"
                                      method="post"
                                      class="mp-deliver-form"

                                    @Html.AntiForgeryToken()
                                    <button type="submit" class="mp-deliver-btn">
                                        <svg viewBox="0 0 20 20" fill="currentColor" width="14" height="14" aria-hidden="true">
                                            <path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M16.704 4.153a.75.75 0 01.143 1.052l-8 10.5a.75.75 0 01-1.127.075l-4.5-4.5a.75.75 0 011.06-1.06l3.894 3.893 7.48-9.817a.75.75 0 011.05-.143z" clip-rule="evenodd" />
                                        </svg>
                                        I have received this item
                                    </button>
                                </form>
                            }
                        </div>

                        <div class="mp-row__price-col">
                            <span class="mp-row__price">₱@order.FinalPrice.ToString("N2")</span>
                            <span class="mp-row__price-label">Final price</span>
                        </div>

                    </article>
                }
            </div>
        }

    </div>

            </div>
        }

            </div>

            <h1 style="font-size: 1.875rem; font-weight: 700;">Active Delivery</h1>
            <p style="color: #6b7280; margin-top: 0.5rem;">Your current delivery status and actions.</p>
        </div>

        {
            <div style="text-align: center; padding: 4rem 2rem; background: #f9fafb; border-radius: 1rem;">
                <p style="font-size: 1.125rem; color: #6b7280;">No active delivery found.</p>
                <a asp-action="Index" style="color: #3b82f6; text-decoration: none; margin-top: 1rem; display: inline-block;">Browse available jobs</a>
            </div>
        }
        else
        {
            var order = Model.Order;
            var item = order?.Item;
            
            <div style="background: white; border: 1px solid #e5e7eb; border-radius: 0.75rem; padding: 1.5rem; margin-bottom: 1.5rem;">
                <div style="margin-bottom: 1rem;">
                    <span style="display: inline-block; padding: 0.25rem 0.75rem; border-radius: 9999px; font-size: 0.875rem; font-weight: 500;
                        @(Model.Status == ThriftLoop.Enums.DeliveryStatus.Accepted ? "background: #fef3c7; color: #92400e;" :
                                                    Model.Status == ThriftLoop.Enums.DeliveryStatus.PickedUp ? "background: #dbeafe; color: #1e40af;" :
                                                    Model.Status == ThriftLoop.Enums.DeliveryStatus.Delivered ? "background: #d1fae5; color: #065f46;" : "background: #e5e7eb; color: #374151;")">
                        Status: @Model.Status
                    </span>
                </div>

                    @(item?.Title ?? "Item #" + order?.ItemId)

                    Category: @(item?.Category ?? "N/A")
                </p>
                
                <p style="color: #6b7280; margin-bottom: 0.5rem;">
                    Buyer: @(order?.Buyer?.Email?.Split('@')[0] ?? "N/A")
                </p>
                
                <p style="color: #6b7280; margin-bottom: 0.5rem;">
                    Buyer Contact: @(order?.Buyer?.Email ?? "N/A")
                </p>
                
                <p style="color: #6b7280; margin-bottom: 0.5rem;">
                    Seller: @(order?.Seller?.Email?.Split('@')[0] ?? "N/A")
                </p>
                
                <p style="font-size: 1.125rem; font-weight: 600; color: #059669; margin-top: 0.5rem;">
                    ₱@(order?.FinalPrice.ToString("N2") ?? "0.00")
                </p>

                    Payment Method: @(order?.PaymentMethod)
                </p>
            </div>

                @if (Model.Status == ThriftLoop.Enums.DeliveryStatus.Accepted)
                {
                    <form asp-action="MarkPickedUp" asp-controller="Rider" method="post">
                        @Html.AntiForgeryToken()
                        <input type="hidden" name="deliveryId" value="@Model.Id" />
                        <button type="submit" style="background: #3b82f6; color: white; border: none; padding: 0.75rem 1.5rem; border-radius: 0.5rem; font-weight: 500; cursor: pointer;">
                            Mark as Picked Up
                        </button>
                    </form>
                }
                
                @if (Model.Status == ThriftLoop.Enums.DeliveryStatus.PickedUp)
                {
                    <form asp-action="MarkDelivered" asp-controller="Rider" method="post">
                        @Html.AntiForgeryToken()
                        <input type="hidden" name="deliveryId" value="@Model.Id" />
                        <button type="submit" style="background: #059669; color: white; border: none; padding: 0.75rem 1.5rem; border-radius: 0.5rem; font-weight: 500; cursor: pointer;">
                            Mark as Delivered
                        </button>
                    </form>
                }
                
                @if (Model.Status == ThriftLoop.Enums.DeliveryStatus.Delivered)
                {
                    <div style="background: #fef3c7; padding: 0.75rem 1.5rem; border-radius: 0.5rem;">
                        <p style="color: #92400e; margin: 0;">Awaiting buyer confirmation</p>
                    </div>
                }
                
                @if (Model.Status == ThriftLoop.Enums.DeliveryStatus.Completed)
                {
                    <div style="background: #d1fae5; padding: 0.75rem 1.5rem; border-radius: 0.5rem;">
                        <p style="color: #065f46; margin: 0;">Delivery completed successfully!</p>
                    </div>
                }
            </div>
            
            <div style="margin-top: 2rem;">
                <a asp-action="Index" style="color: #6b7280; text-decoration: none;">← Back to Dashboard</a>
            </div>
        }
    </main>

@model ThriftLoop.DTOs.Auth.RiderEditDTO
@{
    ViewData["Title"] = "Edit Rider Application";
    Layout = null;
}

<!DOCTYPE html>
<html lang="en">

    <script src="https://cdnjs.cloudflare.com/ajax/libs/jquery/3.6.0/jquery.min.js"></script>
    <script src="https://cdnjs.cloudflare.com/ajax/libs/jquery-validate/1.19.5/jquery.validate.min.js"></script>
    <script src="https://cdnjs.cloudflare.com/ajax/libs/jquery-validation-unobtrusive/3.2.12/jquery.validate.unobtrusive.min.js"></script>
    <script>
        function togglePassword(inputId) {
            const input = document.getElementById(inputId);
            input.type = input.type === 'password' ? 'text' : 'password';
        }

        function previewLicense(input) {
            const preview = document.getElementById('licensePreview');
            const body = document.getElementById('licenseUploadBody');
            if (input.files && input.files[0]) {
                if (input.files[0].size > 5 * 1024 * 1024) {
                    alert('File exceeds 5 MB. Please choose a smaller image.');
                    input.value = '';
                    return;
                }
                const reader = new FileReader();
                reader.onload = function(e) {
                    preview.src = e.target.result;
                    preview.style.display = 'block';
                    body.style.display = 'none';
                };
                reader.readAsDataURL(input.files[0]);
            } else {
                preview.style.display = 'none';
                body.style.display = 'flex';
            }
        }

        document.querySelector('[name="LicensePlate"]')
            ?.addEventListener('blur', function() { this.value = this.value.toUpperCase(); });
    </script>
</body>
</html>

--- Views/Rider/History.cshtml ---
@model IReadOnlyList<ThriftLoop.Models.Delivery>
@{
    ViewData["Title"] = "Delivery History";
    Layout = null;
}

<!DOCTYPE html>
<html lang="en">
<head>
    <meta charset="utf-8" />
    <meta name="viewport" content="width=device-width, initial-scale=1.0" />
    <title>@ViewData["Title"] - ThriftLoop</title>
    <link rel="preconnect" href="https://fonts.googleapis.com">
    <link rel="preconnect" href="https://fonts.gstatic.com" crossorigin>
    <link href="https://fonts.googleapis.com/css2?family=DM+Sans:wght@400;500;600;700&display=swap" rel="stylesheet">
    <link rel="stylesheet" href="~/css/site.css" asp-append-version="true" />
    <link rel="stylesheet" href="~/css/Navbar.css" asp-append-version="true" />
</head>
<body>
    <partial name="_Navbar" />

    <main class="container" style="max-width: 1280px; margin: 2rem auto; padding: 0 1rem;">
        
        <div style="margin-bottom: 2rem;">
            <h1 style="font-size: 1.875rem; font-weight: 700;">Delivery History</h1>
            <p style="color: #6b7280; margin-top: 0.5rem;">All deliveries you've completed or participated in.</p>
        </div>

        @if (!Model.Any())
        {
            <div style="text-align: center; padding: 4rem 2rem; background: #f9fafb; border-radius: 1rem;">
                <p style="font-size: 1.125rem; color: #6b7280;">No delivery history found.</p>
                <a asp-action="Index" asp-controller="Rider" style="color: #3b82f6; text-decoration: none; margin-top: 1rem; display: inline-block;">Browse available jobs</a>
            </div>
        }
        else
        {
            <div style="display: flex; flex-direction: column; gap: 1rem;">
                @foreach (var delivery in Model)
                {
                    var order = delivery.Order;
                    var item = order?.Item;
                    
                    // Determine completion time (prefer buyer confirmation, then rider delivery, then pickup)
                    DateTime? completionTime = delivery.ConfirmedByBuyerAt ?? delivery.DeliveredAt ?? delivery.PickedUpAt;
                    
                    <div style="background: white; border: 1px solid #e5e7eb; border-radius: 0.75rem; padding: 1.5rem;">
                        <div style="display: flex; justify-content: space-between; align-items: flex-start;">
                            <div>
                                <h3 style="font-size: 1.125rem; font-weight: 600; margin-bottom: 0.5rem;">
                                    @(item?.Title ?? "Item #" + order?.ItemId)
                                </h3>
                                <p style="color: #6b7280; font-size: 0.875rem;">
                                    Status: @delivery.Status
                                </p>
                                <p style="color: #6b7280; font-size: 0.875rem;">
                                    Accepted: @(delivery.AcceptedAt?.ToString("MMM d, yyyy") ?? "N/A")
                                </p>
                                <p style="color: #6b7280; font-size: 0.875rem;">
                                    Completed: @(completionTime?.ToString("MMM d, yyyy") ?? "In Progress")
                                </p>
                                @if (delivery.Status == ThriftLoop.Enums.DeliveryStatus.Completed)
                                {
                                    <p style="color: #059669; font-size: 0.875rem; font-weight: 500;">
                                        ✓ Buyer confirmed receipt
                                    </p>
                                }
                            </div>
                            <div>
                                <span style="font-size: 1.125rem; font-weight: 600; color: #059669;">
                                    ₱@(order?.FinalPrice.ToString("N2") ?? "0.00")
                                </span>
                            </div>
                        </div>
                    </div>
                }
            </div>
        }
        
        <div style="margin-top: 2rem;">
            <a asp-action="Index" asp-controller="Rider" style="color: #3b82f6; text-decoration: none;">← Back to Dashboard</a>
        </div>
    </main>
</body>
</html>

--- Views/Rider/Index.cshtml ---
@model IReadOnlyList<ThriftLoop.Models.Delivery>
@{
    ViewData["Title"] = "Rider Dashboard";
    var riderName = ViewBag.RiderName as string ?? "Rider";
    Layout = null;
}

<!DOCTYPE html>
<html lang="en">
<head>
    <meta charset="utf-8" />
    <meta name="viewport" content="width=device-width, initial-scale=1.0" />
    <title>@ViewData["Title"] - ThriftLoop</title>
    <link rel="preconnect" href="https://fonts.googleapis.com">
    <link rel="preconnect" href="https://fonts.gstatic.com" crossorigin>
    <link href="https://fonts.googleapis.com/css2?family=DM+Sans:wght@400;500;600;700&display=swap" rel="stylesheet">
    <link rel="stylesheet" href="~/css/site.css" asp-append-version="true" />
    <link rel="stylesheet" href="~/css/Navbar.css" asp-append-version="true" />
</head>
<body>
    <partial name="_Navbar" />

    <main class="container" style="max-width: 1280px; margin: 2rem auto; padding: 0 1rem;">
        
        @if (TempData["SuccessMessage"] is string successMsg)
        {
            <div style="background: #d1fae5; color: #065f46; padding: 1rem; border-radius: 0.5rem; margin-bottom: 1rem;">
                @successMsg
            </div>
        }
        
        @if (TempData["ErrorMessage"] is string errMsg)
        {
            <div style="background: #fee2e2; color: #991b1b; padding: 1rem; border-radius: 0.5rem; margin-bottom: 1rem;">
                @errMsg
            </div>
        }

        <div style="margin-bottom: 2rem;">
            <h1 style="font-size: 1.875rem; font-weight: 700;">Welcome, @riderName!</h1>
            <p style="color: #6b7280; margin-top: 0.5rem;">Available deliveries are shown below. Accept one to start earning.</p>
        </div>

        @if (!Model.Any())
        {
            <div style="text-align: center; padding: 4rem 2rem; background: #f9fafb; border-radius: 1rem;">
                <p style="font-size: 1.125rem; color: #6b7280;">No deliveries available at the moment.</p>
                <p style="color: #9ca3af; margin-top: 0.5rem;">Check back later for new jobs.</p>
            </div>
        }
        else
        {
            <div style="display: flex; flex-direction: column; gap: 1rem;">
                @foreach (var delivery in Model)
                {
                    var order = delivery.Order;
                    var item = order?.Item;
                    var itemPrice = (order?.FinalPrice ?? 0m) - (order?.DeliveryFee ?? 0m);

                    <div style="background: white; border: 1px solid #e5e7eb; border-radius: 0.75rem; padding: 1.5rem;">
                        <div style="display: flex; justify-content: space-between; align-items: flex-start;">
                            <div>
                                <h3 style="font-size: 1.25rem; font-weight: 600; margin-bottom: 0.5rem;">
                                    @(item?.Title ?? "Item #" + order?.ItemId)
                                </h3>
                                <p style="color: #6b7280; margin-bottom: 0.5rem;">
                                    Category: @(item?.Category ?? "N/A")
                                </p>
                                <p style="color: #6b7280; margin-bottom: 0.5rem;">
                                    Buyer: @(order?.Buyer?.Email?.Split('@')[0] ?? "N/A")
                                </p>
                                <p style="color: #6b7280; margin-bottom: 0.5rem;">
                                    Seller: @(order?.Seller?.Email?.Split('@')[0] ?? "N/A")
                                </p>
                                <p style="color: #6b7280; margin-bottom: 0.25rem;">
                                    Payment: @(order?.PaymentMethod.ToString() ?? "N/A")
                                </p>

                                <div style="margin-top: 0.75rem; padding: 0.75rem; background: #f9fafb; border-radius: 0.5rem; display: inline-block; min-width: 200px;">
                                    <div style="display: flex; justify-content: space-between; gap: 2rem; color: #6b7280; font-size: 0.875rem;">
                                        <span>Item price</span>
                                        <span>₱@itemPrice.ToString("N2")</span>
                                    </div>
                                    <div style="display: flex; justify-content: space-between; gap: 2rem; color: #059669; font-size: 0.875rem; font-weight: 600; margin-top: 0.25rem;">
                                        <span>Your delivery fee</span>
                                        <span>₱@((order?.DeliveryFee ?? 0m).ToString("N2"))</span>
                                    </div>
                                    <div style="border-top: 1px solid #e5e7eb; margin-top: 0.5rem; padding-top: 0.5rem; display: flex; justify-content: space-between; gap: 2rem; font-weight: 600; font-size: 0.9375rem;">
                                        <span>Order total</span>
                                        <span>₱@((order?.FinalPrice ?? 0m).ToString("N2"))</span>
                                    </div>
                                </div>

                                <p style="font-size: 0.875rem; color: #9ca3af; margin-top: 0.75rem;">
                                    Order placed: @(order?.OrderDate.ToString("MMM d, yyyy") ?? "Unknown")
                                </p>
                            </div>
                            <div>
                                <form asp-action="AcceptJob" asp-controller="Rider" method="post">
                                    @Html.AntiForgeryToken()
                                    <input type="hidden" name="deliveryId" value="@delivery.Id" />
                                    <button type="submit" style="background: #3b82f6; color: white; border: none; padding: 0.5rem 1.5rem; border-radius: 0.5rem; font-weight: 500; cursor: pointer;">
                                        Accept Job
                                    </button>
                                </form>
                            </div>
                        </div>
                    </div>
                }
            </div>
        }
    </main>
</body>

--- Views/Sellers/Index.cshtml ---
@model ThriftLoop.ViewModels.SellersViewModel
@using ThriftLoop.Models
@using ThriftLoop.ViewModels
@using ThriftLoop.Enums
@using System.Text.Json
@{
    ViewData["Title"] = "Sellers";
    Layout = null;

    var maxPrice = Model.Items.Any() ? (int)Math.Ceiling((double)Model.Items.Max(i => i.Price)) : 100000;
    ViewBag.MaxPrice = maxPrice;
}

<!DOCTYPE html>
<html lang="en">
<head>
    <meta charset="utf-8" />
    <meta name="viewport" content="width=device-width, initial-scale=1.0" />
    <title>@ViewData["Title"] - ThriftLoop</title>
    <link rel="preconnect" href="https://fonts.googleapis.com">
    <link rel="preconnect" href="https://fonts.gstatic.com" crossorigin>
    <link href="https://fonts.googleapis.com/css2?family=DM+Sans:wght@400;500;600;700&display=swap" rel="stylesheet">
    <link rel="stylesheet" href="~/css/Sellers.css" asp-append-version="true" />
    <link rel="stylesheet" href="~/css/Navbar.css" asp-append-version="true" />
    <link rel="stylesheet" href="~/css/Filter.css" asp-append-version="true" />
</head>
<body>
    @await Html.PartialAsync("_Navbar")
    @await Html.PartialAsync("_Filter")

    <div class="container">
        <main class="fy-main" id="fyMain">
            <header class="fy-feed-header">
                <h1 class="fy-feed-title">Sellers</h1>
                <p class="fy-feed-meta" id="feedMeta">
                    <span id="visibleCount">@Model.Items.Count</span>&nbsp;listings
                </p>
            </header>

            @* Shop suggestion row *@
            @if (Model.Shops.Any())
            {
                <div class="sl-shops-section">
                    <p class="sl-shops-section__label">Shops</p>
                    <div class="sl-shops-row" id="shopsRow">
                        @foreach (var shop in Model.Shops)
                        {

                                   asp-route-id="@shop.Id"

            @if (!Model.Items.Any())

                <div class="fy-empty" id="globalEmpty">

                <div class="fy-empty fy-empty--hidden" id="filterEmpty" aria-live="polite">
                    <div class="fy-empty__icon" aria-hidden="true">
                        <svg viewBox="0 0 64 64" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="1.4">
                            <circle cx="28" cy="28" r="18" />
                            <path d="M42 42l14 14" stroke-linecap="round" />

                <div class="fy-grid" id="itemGrid">

                            {

                                    <a asp-controller="Shop" asp-action="Edit"
                                           asp-route-id="@item.Id"

                                        Manage listing
                                    </a>
                                </div>
                            }
                        </article>
                    }
                </div>
            }
        </main>
    </div>

    <script>
            (function() {
                var grid = document.getElementById('itemGrid');
                var shopsRow = document.getElementById('shopsRow');
                var filterEmpty = document.getElementById('filterEmpty');
                var visibleCount = document.getElementById('visibleCount');

                if (!grid) return;

                var cards = Array.prototype.slice.call(grid.querySelectorAll('.fy-card'));
                var shopCards = shopsRow ? Array.prototype.slice.call(shopsRow.querySelectorAll('.sl-shop-card')) : [];

                // Multi-image hover cycling
                cards.forEach(function(card) {
                    var wrap = card.querySelector('.fy-card__img-wrap');
                    var img = card.querySelector('.fy-card__img');
                    var dotsEl = card.querySelector('.fy-card__dots');

                    if (!wrap || !img) return;

                    var raw = wrap.getAttribute('data-images');
                    var images = [];
                    try { images = JSON.parse(raw); } catch (e) { }
                    if (images.length < 2) return;

                    var dots = dotsEl ? Array.prototype.slice.call(dotsEl.querySelectorAll('.fy-card__dot')) : [];
                    var current = 0;
                    var timer = null;

                    function goTo(idx) {
                        img.classList.add('fy-img--fading');
                        setTimeout(function() {
                            img.src = images[idx];
                            img.classList.remove('fy-img--fading');
                        }, 220);
                        dots.forEach(function(d, i) {
                            d.classList.toggle('fy-card__dot--active', i === idx);
                        });
                        current = idx;
                    }

                    card.addEventListener('mouseenter', function() {
                        if (timer) return;
                        timer = setInterval(function() { goTo((current + 1) % images.length); }, 900);
                    });
                    card.addEventListener('mouseleave', function() {
                        if (timer) { clearInterval(timer); timer = null; }
                        if (current !== 0) goTo(0);
                    });
                });

                // Filter callback
                window.applyFiltersCallback = function(state) {
                    var query = state.search.toLowerCase();
                    var minVal = state.priceMin;
                    var maxVal = state.priceMax;
                    var activeCats = state.categories;
                    var activeConds = state.conditions;

                    var shown = 0;

                    cards.forEach(function(card) {
                        var cat = card.dataset.category;
                        var cond = card.dataset.condition;
                        var price = parseFloat(card.dataset.price);
                        var title = card.dataset.title || '';
                        var desc = card.dataset.desc || '';
                        var shop = card.dataset.shop || '';

                        var catOk = activeCats.length === 0 || activeCats.indexOf(cat) !== -1;
                        var condOk = activeConds.length === 0 || activeConds.indexOf(cond) !== -1;
                        var priceOk = price >= minVal && price <= maxVal;
                        var textOk = !query || title.indexOf(query) !== -1 || desc.indexOf(query) !== -1 || shop.indexOf(query) !== -1;

                        var visible = catOk && condOk && priceOk && textOk;
                        card.classList.toggle('fy-card--hidden', !visible);
                        if (visible) shown++;
                    });

                    // Filter shop cards
                    shopCards.forEach(function(sc) {
                        var name = sc.dataset.shopName || '';
                        sc.classList.toggle('sl-shop-card--hidden',
                            query.length > 0 && name.indexOf(query) === -1);
                    });

                    if (visibleCount) visibleCount.textContent = shown;
                    if (filterEmpty) filterEmpty.classList.toggle('fy-empty--hidden', shown > 0);
                };

                // Reset button inside empty state
                var resetBtn2 = document.getElementById('resetFilters2');
                if (resetBtn2) {
                    resetBtn2.addEventListener('click', function() {
                        if (window.resetFiltersFromPartial) {
                            window.resetFiltersFromPartial();
                        }
                    });
                }
            }());
    </script>
</body>
</html>

@model ErrorViewModel
@{
    ViewData["Title"] = "Error";
}

<h1 class="text-danger">Error.</h1>
<h2 class="text-danger">An error occurred while processing your request.</h2>

@if (Model.ShowRequestId)
{
    <p>
        <strong>Request ID:</strong> <code>@Model.RequestId</code>
    </p>
}

<h3>Development Mode</h3>
<p>
    Swapping to <strong>Development</strong> environment will display more detailed information about the error that occurred.
</p>
<p>
    <strong>The Development environment shouldn't be enabled for deployed applications.</strong>
    It can result in displaying sensitive information from exceptions to end users.
    For local debugging, enable the <strong>Development</strong> environment by setting the <strong>ASPNETCORE_ENVIRONMENT</strong> environment variable to <strong>Development</strong>
    and restarting the app.
</p>


--- Views/Shared/_AddressInputWithMap.cshtml ---
@* Views/Shared/_AddressInputWithMap.cshtml
   ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
   Reusable address field that includes a "Pick on Map" button.
   Drop this partial wherever you have an address <textarea>.

   REQUIRED ViewData keys
   ───────────────────────
   FieldId       (string)  — id & name attr of the <textarea>, e.g. "Address"
   FieldName     (string)  — form field name (usually same as FieldId)
   Label         (string)  — visible label text, e.g. "Address"
   CurrentValue  (string)  — pre-populated value (Model.Address, dto.StoreAddress, …)

   OPTIONAL ViewData keys
   ───────────────────────
   Placeholder   (string)  — textarea placeholder
   HintText      (string)  — small hint rendered below the field
   HasError      (bool)    — whether to apply error styling
   ErrorMessage  (string)  — validation error message to display

   EXAMPLE (User profile page)
   ────────────────────────────
   @{
       var addrError = ViewData.ModelState.ContainsKey("Address")
                       && ViewData.ModelState["Address"]!.Errors.Count > 0;
   }
@using System.Globalization
@using System
   @await Html.PartialAsync("_AddressInputWithMap", (object?)null,
       new ViewDataDictionary(ViewData)
       {
           { "FieldId",      "Address" },
           { "FieldName",    "Address" },
           { "Label",        "Address" },
           { "CurrentValue", Model?.Address ?? string.Empty },
           { "Placeholder",  "Street, Barangay, City/Municipality, Province" },
           { "HintText",     "Your delivery address for purchases" },
           { "HasError",     addrError },
           { "ErrorMessage", addrError
                             ? ViewData.ModelState["Address"]!.Errors[0].ErrorMessage
                             : string.Empty }
       })

   EXAMPLE (Seller application — StoreAddress)
   ─────────────────────────────────────────────
   @await Html.PartialAsync("_AddressInputWithMap", (object?)null,
       new ViewDataDictionary(ViewData)
       {
           { "FieldId",      "StoreAddress" },
           { "FieldName",    "StoreAddress" },
           { "Label",        "Store / Pickup Address" },
           { "CurrentValue", Model?.StoreAddress ?? string.Empty },
           { "Placeholder",  "Full store address visible to buyers" },
           { "HintText",     "This address will be shown on your shop page" },
           { "HasError",     false },
           { "ErrorMessage", string.Empty }
       })

   PREREQUISITES (add to the host page's <head> / end-of-body)
   ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
   In <head>:
       <link rel="stylesheet"
             href="https://unpkg.com/leaflet@1.9.4/dist/leaflet.css" />
       <link rel="stylesheet" href="~/css/map-picker.css" asp-append-version="true" />

   Before </body>:
       @await Html.PartialAsync("_AddressMapModal")
       <script src="https://unpkg.com/leaflet@1.9.4/dist/leaflet.js"></script>
       <script src="~/js/map-picker.js" asp-append-version="true"></script>
   ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
*@
@{
    var fieldId = ViewData["FieldId"] as string ?? "Address";
    var fieldName = ViewData["FieldName"] as string ?? "Address";
    var label = ViewData["Label"] as string ?? "Address";
    var currentValue = ViewData["CurrentValue"] as string ?? string.Empty;
    var placeholder = ViewData["Placeholder"] as string ?? string.Empty;
    var hintText = ViewData["HintText"] as string ?? string.Empty;
    var hasError = ViewData["HasError"] is bool b && b;
    var errorMessage = ViewData["ErrorMessage"] as string ?? string.Empty;

    var inputCss = "up-form-input up-form-textarea" + (hasError ? " up-form-input--error" : "");
}

<div class="up-form-group">
    <label for="@fieldId" class="up-form-label">@label</label>

    <div class="map-input-wrapper">
        <textarea id="@fieldId"
                  name="@fieldName"
                  class="@inputCss"
                  rows="3"
                  placeholder="@placeholder"
                  aria-describedby="@(fieldId)-hint @(fieldId)-error">@currentValue</textarea>

        @* Hidden fields to store the selected coordinates from the map picker *@
        @{ 
            var latKey = $"{fieldId}-Latitude";
            var lngKey = $"{fieldId}-Longitude";

            string? viewDataLat = null;
            if (ViewData[latKey] is not null)
                viewDataLat = ViewData[latKey].ToString();
            else if (ViewData["Latitude"] is not null)
                viewDataLat = ViewData["Latitude"].ToString();

            string? viewDataLng = null;
            if (ViewData[lngKey] is not null)
                viewDataLng = ViewData[lngKey].ToString();
            else if (ViewData["Longitude"] is not null)
                viewDataLng = ViewData["Longitude"].ToString();

            var latVal = viewDataLat
                         ?? (ViewBag.Profile?.Latitude is decimal lat ? lat.ToString(System.Globalization.CultureInfo.InvariantCulture) : ViewBag.Profile?.Latitude?.ToString())
                         ?? string.Empty;
            var lngVal = viewDataLng
                         ?? (ViewBag.Profile?.Longitude is decimal lng ? lng.ToString(System.Globalization.CultureInfo.InvariantCulture) : ViewBag.Profile?.Longitude?.ToString())
                         ?? string.Empty;
        }

        <input type="hidden" id="@(fieldId)-latitude" name="Latitude" value="@latVal" />
        <input type="hidden" id="@(fieldId)-longitude" name="Longitude" value="@lngVal" />

        <button type="button"
                class="map-pick-btn"
                onclick="openMapPicker('@fieldId')"
                title="Pick location on map"
                aria-label="Pick @label on map">
            <svg width="15" height="15" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none"
                 stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round"
                 stroke-linejoin="round" aria-hidden="true">
                <path d="M21 10c0 7-9 13-9 13S3 17 3 10a9 9 0 0 1 18 0z" />
                <circle cx="12" cy="10" r="3" />
            </svg>
            <span>Map</span>
        </button>
    </div>

    @if (hasError && !string.IsNullOrEmpty(errorMessage))
    {
        <span id="@(fieldId)-error" class="up-form-error">@errorMessage</span>
    }

    @if (!string.IsNullOrEmpty(hintText))
    {
        <span id="@(fieldId)-hint" class="up-form-hint">@hintText</span>
    }
</div>

--- Views/Shared/_AddressMapModal.cshtml ---
@* Views/Shared/_AddressMapModal.cshtml
   ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
   Reusable Leaflet address-picker modal.

   USAGE — render ONCE per page, anywhere inside <body>:
       @await Html.PartialAsync("_AddressMapModal")

   The modal is controlled entirely by map-picker.js:
     openMapPicker(inputId)  — opens and targets a <textarea>
     closeMapPicker()        — closes without saving
     confirmMapAddress()     — copies geocoded address and closes
     searchMapAddress()      — forward-geocodes the search query
   ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
*@

<div id="map-picker-modal" class="map-modal-overlay" role="dialog"
     aria-modal="true" aria-labelledby="map-modal-title">

    <div class="map-modal">

        @* ── Header ──────────────────────────────────────────────── *@
        <div class="map-modal__header">
            <span id="map-modal-title" class="map-modal__title">
                <svg width="18" height="18" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none"
                     stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round"
                     stroke-linejoin="round" aria-hidden="true">
                    <path d="M21 10c0 7-9 13-9 13S3 17 3 10a9 9 0 0 1 18 0z" />
                    <circle cx="12" cy="10" r="3" />
                </svg>
                Pick Address on Map
            </span>
            <button type="button" class="map-modal__close"
                    onclick="closeMapPicker()" aria-label="Close map picker">
                <svg width="18" height="18" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none"
                     stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round"
                     stroke-linejoin="round" aria-hidden="true">
                    <line x1="18" y1="6" x2="6" y2="18" />
                    <line x1="6" y1="6" x2="18" y2="18" />
                </svg>
            </button>
        </div>

        @* ── Search bar ───────────────────────────────────────────── *@
        <div id="map-picker-search-wrapper" class="map-modal__search">
            <div class="map-search-wrapper">
                <svg class="map-search-icon" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24"
                     fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2"
                     stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" aria-hidden="true">
                    <circle cx="11" cy="11" r="8" />
                    <line x1="21" y1="21" x2="16.65" y2="16.65" />
                </svg>
                <input id="map-picker-search"
                       type="text"
                       class="map-search-input"
                       placeholder="Search for an address or place…"
                       autocomplete="off"
                       aria-label="Search address" />
                <button type="button" class="map-search-btn" onclick="searchMapAddress()">
                    Search
                </button>
            </div>
        </div>

        @* ── Map ──────────────────────────────────────────────────── *@
        <div class="map-modal__map">
            <div class="map-click-hint" aria-hidden="true">
                Click the map to drop a pin
            </div>
            <div id="map-picker-map" aria-label="Address selection map"></div>
        </div>

        @* ── Geocoded address preview ──────────────────────────────── *@
        <div class="map-modal__result">
            <p class="map-result-label">Selected Address</p>
            <textarea id="map-picker-address-preview"
                      class="map-address-preview"
                      rows="2"
                      placeholder="Click the map or search to select an address…"
                      aria-label="Selected address preview"></textarea>
        </div>

        @* ── Footer ───────────────────────────────────────────────── *@
        <div id="map-picker-footer" class="map-modal__footer">

            <div id="map-geocode-spinner" class="map-geocode-spinner"
                 aria-live="polite" aria-label="Loading address">
                <div class="map-spinner-dot"></div>
                <div class="map-spinner-dot"></div>
                <div class="map-spinner-dot"></div>
                <span>Fetching address…</span>
            </div>

            <button type="button" class="up-btn up-btn--outline" onclick="closeMapPicker()">
                Cancel
            </button>
            <button id="map-picker-confirm-btn" type="button" class="up-btn up-btn--primary" onclick="confirmMapAddress()">

                     stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2.5" stroke-linecap="round"
                     stroke-linejoin="round" aria-hidden="true">

                Use This Address
            </button>
        </div>

    </div>

                Withdrawals
            </a>
            <a asp-controller="Admin" asp-action="SellerApprovals" class="tl-admin-sidebar__link @(currentPath.StartsWith("/Admin/SellerApprovals", StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase) ? "tl-admin-sidebar__link--active" : "")">
                Seller Approvals
            </a>
            <a asp-controller="Admin" asp-action="RiderApprovals" class="tl-admin-sidebar__link @(currentPath.StartsWith("/Admin/RiderApprovals", StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase) ? "tl-admin-sidebar__link--active" : "")">
                Rider Approvals
            </a>
        </nav>

        <form asp-action="Logout" asp-controller="Auth" method="post" class="tl-admin-sidebar__logout">
            @Html.AntiForgeryToken()
            <button type="submit" class="tl-admin-sidebar__logout-btn">Sign out</button>
        </form>
    </aside>
}


--- Views/Shared/_Filter.cshtml ---
@using ThriftLoop.ViewModels
@using ThriftLoop.Enums
@{
    var categories = ItemCreateViewModel.Categories;
    var conditions = ItemCreateViewModel.Conditions;
    var maxPrice = ViewBag.MaxPrice ?? 100000;
}

<aside class="floating-filter" id="floatingFilter" aria-label="Filter listings">
    <div class="floating-filter__header">
        <span class="floating-filter__title">Filters</span>
        <button type="button" class="floating-filter__reset" id="resetFilters">Clear all</button>
        <button type="button" class="floating-filter__close" id="closeFilter" aria-label="Close filters">
            <svg viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" width="18" height="18">
                <path d="M18 6L6 18M6 6l12 12" stroke-linecap="round" />
            </svg>
        </button>
    </div>

    <div class="floating-filter__content">
        <!-- Search -->
        <div class="floating-filter__group">
            <label class="floating-filter__label" for="searchInput">Search</label>
            <div class="floating-filter__search-wrap">
                <svg viewBox="0 0 20 20" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="1.6" aria-hidden="true">
                    <circle cx="8.5" cy="8.5" r="5.5" />
                    <path d="M13.5 13.5L18 18" stroke-linecap="round" />
                </svg>
                <input type="search" id="searchInput" class="floating-filter__search-input"
                       placeholder="Title, description or shop…" autocomplete="off" />
            </div>
        </div>

        <!-- Price Range -->
        <div class="floating-filter__group">
            <label class="floating-filter__label">Price</label>
            <div class="floating-filter__price-row">
                <div class="floating-filter__price-field">
                    <span class="floating-filter__price-sym">₱</span>
                    <input type="number" id="priceMin" class="floating-filter__price-input"
                           placeholder="0" min="0" max="@maxPrice" value="0" />
                </div>
                <span class="floating-filter__price-sep">–</span>
                <div class="floating-filter__price-field">
                    <span class="floating-filter__price-sym">₱</span>
                    <input type="number" id="priceMax" class="floating-filter__price-input"
                           placeholder="@maxPrice" min="0" max="@maxPrice" value="@maxPrice" />
                </div>
            </div>
        </div>

        <!-- Categories -->
        <div class="floating-filter__group">
            <p class="floating-filter__label">Category</p>
            <ul class="floating-filter__check-list" id="catFilters">
                @foreach (var cat in categories)
                {
                    <li>
                        <label class="floating-filter__check-label">
                            <input type="checkbox" class="floating-filter__check" value="@cat" />
                            <span class="floating-filter__check-box"></span>
                            <span class="floating-filter__check-text">@cat</span>
                        </label>
                    </li>
                }
            </ul>
        </div>

        <!-- Conditions -->
        <div class="floating-filter__group">
            <p class="floating-filter__label">Condition</p>
            <ul class="floating-filter__check-list" id="condFilters">
                @foreach (var cond in conditions)
                {
                    <li>
                        <label class="floating-filter__check-label">
                            <input type="checkbox" class="floating-filter__check" value="@cond" />
                            <span class="floating-filter__check-box"></span>
                            <span class="floating-filter__check-text">@cond</span>
                        </label>
                    </li>
                }
            </ul>
        </div>
    </div>

    <div class="floating-filter__footer">
        <button type="button" class="floating-filter__apply" id="applyFilters">Apply Filters</button>
    </div>
</aside>

<!-- Mobile filter toggle button -->
<button type="button" class="floating-filter__toggle" id="filterToggle" aria-label="Open filters">
    <svg viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="1.8" width="20" height="20">
        <path d="M4 6h16M6 12h12M8 18h8" stroke-linecap="round" />
        <circle cx="8" cy="6" r="2" />
        <circle cx="16" cy="12" r="2" />
        <circle cx="12" cy="18" r="2" />
    </svg>
    <span>Filters</span>
</button>

<script>
    (function() {
        // Initialize filter values from ViewBag
        var maxPriceValue = @maxPrice;
        
        // Store filter state
        var filterState = {
            search: '',
            priceMin: 0,
            priceMax: maxPriceValue,
            categories: [],
            conditions: []
        };
        
        // Get DOM elements
        var searchInput = document.getElementById('searchInput');
        var priceMinInput = document.getElementById('priceMin');
        var priceMaxInput = document.getElementById('priceMax');
        var catChecks = document.querySelectorAll('#catFilters .floating-filter__check');
        var condChecks = document.querySelectorAll('#condFilters .floating-filter__check');
        var applyBtn = document.getElementById('applyFilters');
        var resetBtns = document.querySelectorAll('#resetFilters');
        var filterToggle = document.getElementById('filterToggle');
        var closeFilter = document.getElementById('closeFilter');
        var filterPanel = document.getElementById('floatingFilter');
        
        // Function to capture current filter state
        function captureFilterState() {
            filterState.search = searchInput ? searchInput.value.trim() : '';
            filterState.priceMin = priceMinInput ? parseFloat(priceMinInput.value) || 0 : 0;
            filterState.priceMax = priceMaxInput ? parseFloat(priceMaxInput.value) || maxPriceValue : maxPriceValue;
            filterState.categories = Array.from(catChecks).filter(cb => cb.checked).map(cb => cb.value);
            filterState.conditions = Array.from(condChecks).filter(cb => cb.checked).map(cb => cb.value);
        }
        
        // Function to apply filters to the page (to be overridden by parent page)
        window.applyFiltersFromPartial = function() {
            captureFilterState();
            if (window.applyFiltersCallback) {
                window.applyFiltersCallback(filterState);
            }
        };
        
        // Function to reset filters
        window.resetFiltersFromPartial = function() {
            if (searchInput) searchInput.value = '';
            if (priceMinInput) priceMinInput.value = 0;
            if (priceMaxInput) priceMaxInput.value = maxPriceValue;
            catChecks.forEach(cb => cb.checked = false);
            condChecks.forEach(cb => cb.checked = false);
            applyFiltersFromPartial();
        };
        
        // Event listeners
        if (applyBtn) {
            applyBtn.addEventListener('click', applyFiltersFromPartial);
        }
        
        resetBtns.forEach(btn => {
            btn.addEventListener('click', function(e) {
                e.preventDefault();
                window.resetFiltersFromPartial();
            });
        });
        
        // Mobile toggle
        if (filterToggle && filterPanel) {
            filterToggle.addEventListener('click', function() {
                filterPanel.classList.add('floating-filter--open');
                document.body.style.overflow = 'hidden';
            });
        }
        
        if (closeFilter && filterPanel) {
            closeFilter.addEventListener('click', function() {
                filterPanel.classList.remove('floating-filter--open');
                document.body.style.overflow = '';
            });
        }
        
        // Close filter when clicking outside on mobile
        if (filterPanel) {
            document.addEventListener('click', function(e) {
                if (window.innerWidth <= 768 && filterPanel.classList.contains('floating-filter--open')) {
                    if (!filterPanel.contains(e.target) && !filterToggle.contains(e.target)) {
                        filterPanel.classList.remove('floating-filter--open');
                        document.body.style.overflow = '';
                    }
                }
            });
        }
    })();
</script>

--- Views/Shared/_Navbar.cshtml ---
@using System.Security.Claims
@using ThriftLoop.Repositories.Interface
@inject IShopRepository ShopRepo

@{
    var userEmail = User.FindFirst(ClaimTypes.Email)?.Value
                        ?? User.Identity?.Name
                        ?? string.Empty;
    var displayName = userEmail.Contains('@') ? userEmail.Split('@')[0] : userEmail;
    var currentPath = Context.Request.Path.Value ?? string.Empty;
    
    // Check if current user is a Rider
    var isRider = User.HasClaim(c => c.Type == "IsRider" && c.Value == "true");
    
    // Resolve live shop name for the navbar pill (only for Sellers)
    var shopLabel = "My Shop";
    if (!isRider && User.IsInRole("Seller"))
    {
        var rawId = User.FindFirst(ClaimTypes.NameIdentifier)?.Value;
        if (int.TryParse(rawId, out var navUserId))
        {
            var shop = await ShopRepo.GetByUserIdAsync(navUserId);
            if (!string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(shop?.ShopName))
                shopLabel = shop.ShopName;
        }
    }
}

<nav class="tl-nav">

        }
        else
        {
            <a asp-controller="Home" asp-action="Index" class="tl-nav__logo">ThriftLoop</a>

<script>
    document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function() {
        const dropdownToggle = document.getElementById('userDropdown');
        const dropdownMenu = document.getElementById('userDropdownMenu');

        if (dropdownToggle && dropdownMenu) {
            dropdownToggle.addEventListener('click', function(e) {
                e.preventDefault();
                e.stopPropagation();
                const isExpanded = this.getAttribute('aria-expanded') === 'true';
                this.setAttribute('aria-expanded', !isExpanded);
                dropdownMenu.classList.toggle('show');
            });

            document.addEventListener('click', function(e) {
                if (!dropdownToggle.contains(e.target) && !dropdownMenu.contains(e.target)) {
                    dropdownToggle.setAttribute('aria-expanded', 'false');
                    dropdownMenu.classList.remove('show');
                }
            });
        }
    });
</script>

        crossorigin="anonymous" referrerpolicy="no-referrer"></script>

    ViewData["Title"] = "Add Item — " + Model.ShopName;
    Layout = null;
    var afToken = Antiforgery.GetAndStoreTokens(Context).RequestToken ?? string.Empty;
}

<!DOCTYPE html>

    <title>@ViewData["Title"] - ThriftLoop</title>
    <link rel="preconnect" href="https://fonts.googleapis.com">
    <link rel="preconnect" href="https://fonts.gstatic.com" crossorigin>
    <link href="https://fonts.googleapis.com/css2?family=DM+Sans:ital,opsz,wght@0,9..40,400;0,9..40,500;0,9..40,600;0,9..40,700;1,9..40,400&display=swap" rel="stylesheet">

<body>
    @await Html.PartialAsync("_Navbar")

    <div class="ic-shell">

        <div class="ic-header">
