@* Render map modal and picker for all viewers (view-only or editable depending on openMapPicker args) *@
@await Html.PartialAsync("_AddressMapModal")
<script src="https://unpkg.com/leaflet@1.9.4/dist/leaflet.js"></script>
<script src="~/js/map-picker.js" asp-append-version="true"></script>

    <script>
    (function () {
        'use strict';

        // Attach a simple view-only opener for non-owners so they can see the exact pin
        const isOwnerFlag = @isOwner.ToString().ToLowerInvariant();
        if (isOwnerFlag === 'false') {
            function attachViewClick() {
                const el = document.getElementById('shopAddressDisplay');
                if (!el) return;
                el.style.cursor = 'pointer';
                el.addEventListener('click', async function (e) {
                    e.preventDefault();
                    console.log('[shop] address clicked — attempting to open map picker');
                    try {
                        if (typeof window.openMapPicker === 'function') {
                            window.openMapPicker('ShopLocation', null, 'view');
                            return;
                        }

                        // If map-picker isn't loaded for some reason, load it dynamically then open
                        const scriptUrl = '/js/map-picker.js';
                        await new Promise((resolve, reject) => {
                            const s = document.createElement('script');
                            s.src = scriptUrl;
                            s.async = false;
                            s.onload = resolve;
                            s.onerror = () => reject(new Error('Failed to load ' + scriptUrl));
                            document.head.appendChild(s);
                        });

                        if (typeof window.openMapPicker === 'function') {
                            window.openMapPicker('ShopLocation', null, 'view');
                        } else {
                            console.warn('[shop] openMapPicker still not available after loading script');
                            alert('Map picker is not available.');
                        }
                    } catch (err) {
                        console.warn('Map picker not available', err);
                        alert('Unable to open map picker. See console for details.');
                    }
                });
            }

            if (document.readyState === 'loading') document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', attachViewClick);
            else attachViewClick();
        }
    }());
</script>

@if (isOwner)
{
    <input type="hidden" id="afToken" value="@afToken" />
    <script>
        (function () {
        'use strict';

        const SHOP_ID   = @Model.ShopId;
        const AF_TOKEN  = document.getElementById('afToken').value;
        const FIELD_URL = '/Shop/SaveField';
        const IMAGE_URL = '/Shop/SaveImage';

        // ── AJAX helpers ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────
        async function saveTextField(field, value) {
        const res = await fetch(FIELD_URL, {
        method: 'POST',
        headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json', 'RequestVerificationToken': AF_TOKEN },
        body: JSON.stringify({ shopId: SHOP_ID, field, value })
        });
        return res.json();
        }

        async function uploadImage(field, file) {
        const fd = new FormData();
        fd.append('shopId', SHOP_ID);
        fd.append('field',  field);
        fd.append('file',   file);
        const res = await fetch(IMAGE_URL, {
        method: 'POST',
        headers: { 'RequestVerificationToken': AF_TOKEN },
        body: fd
        });
        return res.json();
        }

        // ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
        //  IMAGE MODAL (unchanged)
        // ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
        const backdrop    = document.getElementById('imgModalBackdrop');
        const modalTitle  = document.getElementById('imgModalTitle');
        const previewArea = document.getElementById('imgPreviewArea');
        const dropZone    = document.getElementById('imgDropZone');
        const fileInput   = document.getElementById('imgFileInput');
        const dropInner   = document.getElementById('imgDropInner');
        const saveBtn     = document.getElementById('imgModalSave');
        const cancelBtn   = document.getElementById('imgModalCancel');
        const closeBtn    = document.getElementById('imgModalClose');
        const errorEl     = document.getElementById('imgModalError');

        let activeField = null;
        let pendingFile = null;

        function openModal(field, currentUrl, title) {
        activeField      = field;
        pendingFile      = null;
        saveBtn.disabled = true;
        errorEl.hidden   = true;
        fileInput.value  = '';
        modalTitle.textContent = title;

        previewArea.innerHTML = '';
        if (currentUrl && currentUrl !== 'null') {
        if (field === 'BannerUrl') {
        const div = document.createElement('div');
        div.className = 'sp-modal__banner-preview';
        const cleanUrl = currentUrl.split('?')[0];
        div.style.backgroundImage = `url('${cleanUrl}')`;
        previewArea.appendChild(div);
        } else {
        const img = document.createElement('img');
        const cleanUrl = currentUrl.split('?')[0];
        img.src = cleanUrl;
        img.className = 'sp-modal__logo-preview';
        previewArea.appendChild(img);
        }
        } else {
        const empty = document.createElement('div');
        empty.className = 'sp-modal__preview-empty';
        empty.textContent = 'No image set — upload one below';
        previewArea.appendChild(empty);
        }

        dropInner.querySelector('.sp-modal__drop-label').textContent = 'Click or drag an image here';
        backdrop.removeAttribute('hidden');
        dropZone.focus();
        }

        function closeModal() {
        backdrop.setAttribute('hidden', '');
        activeField = pendingFile = null;
        }

        closeBtn?.addEventListener('click',  closeModal);
        cancelBtn?.addEventListener('click', closeModal);
        backdrop?.addEventListener('click',  e => { if (e.target === backdrop) closeModal(); });
        document.addEventListener('keydown', e => { if (e.key === 'Escape') closeModal(); });

        function handleFile(file) {
        if (!file) return;
        const allowed = ['image/jpeg','image/png','image/webp','image/gif'];
        if (!allowed.includes(file.type)) { showModalError('Only JPEG, PNG, WebP, or GIF images are allowed.'); return; }
        if (file.size > 5 * 1024 * 1024)  { showModalError('File exceeds the 5 MB limit.'); return; }

        errorEl.hidden     = true;
        pendingFile        = file;
        saveBtn.disabled   = false;

        const reader = new FileReader();
        reader.onload = e => {
        previewArea.innerHTML = '';
        if (activeField === 'BannerUrl') {
        const div = document.createElement('div');
        div.className = 'sp-modal__banner-preview';
        div.style.backgroundImage = `url('${e.target.result}')`;
        previewArea.appendChild(div);
        } else {
        const img = document.createElement('img');
        img.src = e.target.result;
        img.className = 'sp-modal__logo-preview';
        previewArea.appendChild(img);
        }
        };
        reader.readAsDataURL(file);
        dropInner.querySelector('.sp-modal__drop-label').textContent = file.name;
        }

        fileInput?.addEventListener('change', () => handleFile(fileInput.files[0]));
        dropZone?.addEventListener('dragover',  e => { e.preventDefault(); dropZone.classList.add('sp-modal__drop-zone--over'); });
        dropZone?.addEventListener('dragleave', ()  => dropZone.classList.remove('sp-modal__drop-zone--over'));
        dropZone?.addEventListener('drop', e => {
        e.preventDefault();
        dropZone.classList.remove('sp-modal__drop-zone--over');
        handleFile(e.dataTransfer.files[0]);
        });

        saveBtn?.addEventListener('click', async () => {
        if (!pendingFile || !activeField) return;
                
        const originalText = saveBtn.textContent;
        saveBtn.disabled    = true;
        saveBtn.textContent = 'Uploading…';
        errorEl.hidden      = true;

        try {
        const res = await uploadImage(activeField, pendingFile);
                    
        if (!res.ok) {
        showModalError(res.error || 'Upload failed');
        saveBtn.disabled = false;
        saveBtn.textContent = originalText;
        return;
        }

        const cacheBuster = `${res.url}?v=${Date.now()}`;

        if (activeField === 'BannerUrl') {
        const banner = document.getElementById('shopBanner');
        banner.style.backgroundImage = `url('${cacheBuster}')`;
        const placeholder = banner.querySelector('.sp-banner__placeholder');
        if (placeholder) placeholder.remove();
        banner.setAttribute('data-original-bg', res.url);
        } else {
        const existingLogo = document.getElementById('shopLogoImg');
                        
        if (existingLogo) {
        if (existingLogo.tagName === 'DIV') {
        const img = document.createElement('img');
        img.src = cacheBuster;
        img.id = 'shopLogoImg';
        img.alt = 'Shop logo';
        img.className = 'sp-identity__logo';
        img.setAttribute('data-original-src', res.url);
        existingLogo.replaceWith(img);
        } else if (existingLogo.tagName === 'IMG') {
        existingLogo.src = cacheBuster;
        existingLogo.setAttribute('data-original-src', res.url);
        }
        }
        }
                    
        const tempMsg = document.createElement('div');
        tempMsg.textContent = 'Image uploaded successfully!';
        tempMsg.style.cssText = 'position:fixed;bottom:20px;right:20px;background:#0e6245;color:#fff;padding:10px 20px;border-radius:8px;z-index:1000;animation:fadeOut 2s ease forwards;';
        document.body.appendChild(tempMsg);
        setTimeout(() => tempMsg.remove(), 2000);
                    
        } catch (err) {
        showModalError('Network error. Please try again.');
        console.error('Upload error:', err);
        } finally {
        saveBtn.disabled = false;
        saveBtn.textContent = originalText;
        }
                
        closeModal();
        });

        function showModalError(msg) {
        errorEl.textContent = msg;
        errorEl.hidden      = false;
        }

        const bannerElement = document.getElementById('shopBanner');
        if (bannerElement) {
        bannerElement.addEventListener('click', () => {
        const style = bannerElement.style.backgroundImage;
        let current = null;
        if (style && style !== 'none') {
        current = style.replace(/^url\(['"]?/, '').replace(/['"]?\)$/, '').split('?')[0];
        }
        openModal('BannerUrl', current, 'Banner Image');
        });
        }

        const logoWrap = document.getElementById('shopLogoWrap');
        if (logoWrap) {
        const openLogo = () => {
        const img = document.getElementById('shopLogoImg');
        let current = null;
        if (img && img.tagName === 'IMG') {
        current = img.getAttribute('data-original-src') || img.src.split('?')[0];
        }
        openModal('LogoUrl', current, 'Logo Image');
        };
        logoWrap.addEventListener('click', openLogo);
        logoWrap.addEventListener('keydown', e => {
        if (e.key === 'Enter' || e.key === ' ') {
        e.preventDefault();
        openLogo();
        }
        });
        }

        const style = document.createElement('style');
        style.textContent = `
        @@keyframes fadeOut {
        0% { opacity: 1; transform: translateY(0); }
        70% { opacity: 1; transform: translateY(0); }
        100% { opacity: 0; transform: translateY(-20px); visibility: hidden; }
        }
        `;
        document.head.appendChild(style);

        function refreshImagesWithCacheBuster() {
        const logo = document.getElementById('shopLogoImg');
        if (logo && logo.tagName === 'IMG' && logo.src) {
        const originalSrc = logo.getAttribute('data-original-src') || logo.src.split('?')[0];
        if (originalSrc && originalSrc !== '') {
        logo.src = originalSrc + '?v=' + Date.now();
        }
        }
                
        const banner = document.getElementById('shopBanner');
        if (banner && banner.style.backgroundImage) {
        const bg = banner.style.backgroundImage;
        const urlMatch = bg.match(/url\(['"]?([^'"]+)['"]?\)/);
        if (urlMatch && urlMatch[1]) {
        const cleanUrl = urlMatch[1].split('?')[0];
        if (cleanUrl && cleanUrl !== '' && cleanUrl !== 'none') {
        banner.style.backgroundImage = `url('${cleanUrl}?v=${Date.now()}')`;
        }
        }
        }
        }

        if (document.readyState === 'loading') {
        document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', refreshImagesWithCacheBuster);
        } else {
        refreshImagesWithCacheBuster();
        }

        // ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
        //  INLINE TEXT EDITING (ShopName + Bio) - unchanged
        // ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
        document.querySelectorAll('.sp-inline--editable').forEach(block => {
        const display   = block.querySelector('.sp-inline__display');
        const editor    = block.querySelector('.sp-inline__editor');
        const input     = block.querySelector('.sp-inline__input');
        const saveBtn   = block.querySelector('.sp-inline__save');
        const cancelBtn = block.querySelector('.sp-inline__cancel');
        const errorEl   = block.querySelector('.sp-inline__error');
        const field     = block.dataset.field;

        if (!display || !editor || !input) return;

        let originalValue = input.value;

        function openEditor() {
        input.value = originalValue;
        display.hidden = true;
        editor.removeAttribute('hidden');
        block.classList.add('sp-inline--editing');
        input.focus();
        if (input.tagName === 'INPUT')
        input.setSelectionRange(input.value.length, input.value.length);
        }
        function closeEditor(restore) {
        if (restore) input.value = originalValue;
        display.hidden = false;
        editor.setAttribute('hidden', '');
        errorEl.hidden = true;
        block.classList.remove('sp-inline--editing');
        }

        display.addEventListener('click', openEditor);
        cancelBtn.addEventListener('click', () => closeEditor(true));

        input.addEventListener('keydown', e => {
        if (e.key === 'Escape') { e.preventDefault(); closeEditor(true); }
        if ((e.metaKey || e.ctrlKey) && e.key === 'Enter') saveBtn.click();
        });

        saveBtn.addEventListener('click', async () => {
        const val = input.value.trim();
        errorEl.hidden      = true;
        saveBtn.disabled    = true;
        saveBtn.textContent = 'Saving…';

        const res = await saveTextField(field, val);

        saveBtn.disabled    = false;
        saveBtn.textContent = 'Save';

        if (!res.ok) {
        errorEl.textContent = res.error;
        errorEl.hidden      = false;
        return;
        }

        originalValue = val;

        if (field === 'ShopName') {
        const h1 = display;
        const editHint = h1.querySelector('.sp-inline__edit-hint');
        if (editHint) {
        h1.childNodes[0].textContent = val + ' ';
        } else {
        h1.textContent = val;
        }
        document.title = val;
        } else {
        display.textContent = val || 'Click to add a bio…';
        display.classList.toggle('sp-identity__bio--empty', !val);
        if (val) {
        const hint = block.querySelector('.sp-inline__edit-hint');
        if (hint) display.appendChild(hint);
        }
        }

        closeEditor(false);
        });
        });

        // ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
        //  ADDRESS INLINE EDIT (click on address line opens editor with map picker)
        // ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
        const addressContainer = document.querySelector('.sp-address');
        if (addressContainer && addressContainer.classList.contains('sp-inline--editable')) {
        const displayEl = document.getElementById('shopAddressDisplay');
        const editorDiv = addressContainer.querySelector('.sp-address__editor');
        const addressInput = document.getElementById('addressTextInput');
        const saveAddressBtn = addressContainer.querySelector('.sp-address__save');
        const cancelAddressBtn = addressContainer.querySelector('.sp-address__cancel');
        const addressError = addressContainer.querySelector('.sp-address__error');
        const mapPickerBtn = document.getElementById('openMapPickerBtn');
                
        let originalAddress = addressInput?.value || '';

        function openAddressEditor() {
        if (!editorDiv) return;
        originalAddress = addressInput?.value || '';
        displayEl.style.display = 'none';
        editorDiv.removeAttribute('hidden');
        addressInput?.focus();
        }

        function closeAddressEditor(restore) {
        if (restore && addressInput) addressInput.value = originalAddress;
        displayEl.style.display = 'block';
        editorDiv?.setAttribute('hidden', '');
        if (addressError) addressError.hidden = true;
        }

        // Click on address line opens editor
        displayEl?.addEventListener('click', openAddressEditor);

        // Cancel button
        cancelAddressBtn?.addEventListener('click', () => closeAddressEditor(true));

        // Save address (text + lat/lng)
        saveAddressBtn?.addEventListener('click', async () => {
        const newAddress = addressInput?.value.trim() || '';
        if (addressError) addressError.hidden = true;
        saveAddressBtn.disabled = true;
        saveAddressBtn.textContent = 'Saving…';

        // Get current lat/lng from hidden fields
        let lat = document.getElementById('ShopLocation-latitude')?.value || '';
        let lng = document.getElementById('ShopLocation-longitude')?.value || '';

        // Save both address text and coordinates via SaveField?
        // Since the backend expects a single field per call, we save address text first,
        // then coordinates if they changed (map picker would have updated them).
        // For simplicity, we call SaveField for StoreAddress.
        const res = await saveTextField('StoreAddress', newAddress);

        // If saving text failed, show error and stop
        if (!res.ok) {
            saveAddressBtn.disabled = false;
            saveAddressBtn.textContent = 'Save';
            if (addressError) {
                addressError.textContent = res.error || 'Failed to save address';
                addressError.hidden = false;
            }
            return;
        }

        // If we have coordinates, send them via SaveLocation so server persists lat/lng
        try {
            const latNum = lat ? parseFloat(lat) : null;
            const lngNum = lng ? parseFloat(lng) : null;
            if (latNum != null && lngNum != null) {
                const locRes = await fetch('/Shop/SaveLocation', {
                    method: 'POST',
                    headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json', 'RequestVerificationToken': AF_TOKEN },
                    body: JSON.stringify({ shopId: SHOP_ID, latitude: latNum, longitude: lngNum })
                });
                const locJson = await locRes.json();
                if (!locJson.ok) {
                    // non-fatal: show error but keep address text saved
                    if (addressError) {
                        addressError.textContent = locJson.error || 'Failed to save coordinates';
                        addressError.hidden = false;
                    }
                }
            }
        } catch (err) {
            console.warn('Failed to save coordinates', err);
        } finally {
            saveAddressBtn.disabled = false;
            saveAddressBtn.textContent = 'Save';
        }

        // Update displayed address
        displayEl.innerHTML = (newAddress || 'No address set') +
            `<span class="sp-inline__edit-hint" aria-hidden="true">` +
            `<svg viewBox="0 0 16 16" fill="currentColor" width="11" height="11">` +
            `<path d="M11.013 1.427a1.75 1.75 0 012.474 0l1.086 1.086a1.75 1.75 0 010 2.474l-8.61 8.61c-.21.21-.47.364-.756.445l-3.251.93a.75.75 0 01-.927-.928l.929-3.25c.081-.286.235-.547.445-.758l8.61-8.61z" />` +
            `</svg></span>`;
        originalAddress = newAddress;
        closeAddressEditor(false);
        });

        // Map picker integration
        if (mapPickerBtn && typeof window.openMapPicker === 'function') {
        mapPickerBtn.addEventListener('click', (e) => {
        e.preventDefault();
        // Open map picker, after selection it will fill lat/lng hidden inputs and address text field
        window.openMapPicker('ShopLocation', (latLng, addressString) => {
        if (addressInput && addressString) {
        addressInput.value = addressString;
        }
        // The map-picker.js also updates hidden lat/lng inputs
        });
        });
        } else if (mapPickerBtn) {
        // Fallback if map picker not loaded
        console.warn('openMapPicker not available');
        }

        @* For non-owners: clicking the address should open the map in view-only mode *@
        @if (!isOwner)
        {
            <text>
        const shopAddressDisplayView = document.getElementById('shopAddressDisplay');
        shopAddressDisplayView?.addEventListener('click', function (e) {
            e.preventDefault();
            // open in view-only mode so users can see the precise pin (no editing)
            window.openMapPicker('ShopLocation', null, 'view');
        });
            </text>
        }

        // Close on Escape
        document.addEventListener('keydown', (e) => {
        if (e.key === 'Escape' && editorDiv && !editorDiv.hidden) {
        closeAddressEditor(true);
        }
        });
        }

        }());
    </script>
}

<script>
    (function () {
        'use strict';
        var isOwner = @isOwner.ToString().ToLowerInvariant();
        if (!isOwner) {
            function attachViewerAddressClick() {
                var addr = document.getElementById('shopAddressDisplay');
                if (!addr) return;
                addr.style.cursor = 'pointer';
                addr.setAttribute('role', 'button');
                addr.tabIndex = 0;
                addr.addEventListener('click', function (e) {
                    e.preventDefault();
                    try {
                        if (typeof window.openMapPicker === 'function') {
                            window.openMapPicker('ShopLocation', null, 'view');
                            return;
                        }
                        var s = document.createElement('script');
                        s.src = '/js/map-picker.js';
                        s.onload = function () { if (typeof window.openMapPicker === 'function') window.openMapPicker('ShopLocation', null, 'view'); };
                        s.onerror = function () { console.warn('Failed to load map-picker.js'); };
                        document.head.appendChild(s);
                    } catch (err) {
                        console.warn('openMapPicker failed', err);
                    }
                });
                addr.addEventListener('keydown', function (e) { if (e.key === 'Enter' || e.key === ' ') { e.preventDefault(); addr.click(); } });
            }
            if (document.readyState === 'loading') document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', attachViewerAddressClick); else attachViewerAddressClick();
        }
    }());
</script>


--- Views/User/index.cshtml ---
@model ThriftLoop.DTOs.User.UpdateProfileDTO
@using ThriftLoop.Enums
@{
    ViewData["Title"] = "My Profile";
    Layout = null;

    var profile = ViewBag.Profile as ThriftLoop.DTOs.User.UserProfileDTO;
    var sellerApp = ViewBag.SellerApplication as ThriftLoop.DTOs.User.SellerApplicationStatusDTO;

    @* ── Address field validation state ───────────────────────── *@
    var addrError = ViewData.ModelState.ContainsKey("Address")
                    && ViewData.ModelState["Address"]!.Errors.Count > 0;
    var addrErrorMsg = addrError
                       ? ViewData.ModelState["Address"]!.Errors[0].ErrorMessage
                       : string.Empty;
}

<!DOCTYPE html>
<html lang="en">

    <meta charset="utf-8" />
    <meta name="viewport" content="width=device-width, initial-scale=1.0" />
    <title>@ViewData["Title"] - ThriftLoop</title>
    <link rel="preconnect" href="https://fonts.googleapis.com">
    <link rel="preconnect" href="https://fonts.gstatic.com" crossorigin>
    <link href="https://fonts.googleapis.com/css2?family=DM+Sans:wght@400;500;600;700&display=swap" rel="stylesheet">

    @* ── Leaflet + Map Picker ──────────────────────────────────── *@

    <link rel="stylesheet" href="~/css/map-picker.css" asp-append-version="true" />

<body>
    @await Html.PartialAsync("_Navbar")

    <div class="up-container">

            @* ── Left sidebar: user info ───────────────────────────────────────── *@
            <aside class="up-sidebar" aria-label="Profile information">

                <div class="up-profile-card">

                        @(profile?.FullName?.FirstOrDefault().ToString().ToUpper() ?? "U")

                        </span>
                        @if (profile?.IsGoogleAccount == true)

                                    <path d="M12 23c2.97 0 5.46-.98 7.28-2.66l-3.57-2.77c-.98.66-2.23 1.06-3.71 1.06-2.86 0-5.29-1.93-6.16-4.53H2.18v2.84C3.99 20.53 7.7 23 12 23z" />
                                    <path d="M5.84 14.09c-.22-.66-.35-1.36-.35-2.09s.13-1.43.35-2.09V7.07H2.18C1.43 8.55 1 10.22 1 12s.43 3.45 1.18 4.93l2.85-2.22.81-.62z" />
                                    <path d="M12 5.38c1.62 0 3.06.56 4.21 1.64l3.15-3.15C17.45 2.09 14.97 1 12 1 7.7 1 3.99 3.47 2.18 7.07l3.66 2.84c.87-2.6 3.3-4.53 6.16-4.53z" />
                                </svg>
                                Google Account
                            </span>
                        }
                    </div>
                </div>

                <div class="up-filter-group">
                    <span class="up-filter-group__label">Account Information</span>
                    <ul class="up-info-list">
                        <li class="up-info-item">
                            <span class="up-info-label">Email</span>
                            <span class="up-info-value">@profile?.Email</span>
                        </li>
                        <li class="up-info-item">
                            <span class="up-info-label">Member Since</span>
                            <span class="up-info-value">@profile?.CreatedAt.ToString("MMMM d, yyyy")</span>
                        </li>
                        @if (!string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(profile?.PhoneNumber))
                        {
                            <li class="up-info-item">
                                <span class="up-info-label">Phone</span>
                                <span class="up-info-value">@profile?.PhoneNumber</span>
                            </li>
                        }
                        @if (!string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(profile?.Address))
                        {
                            <li class="up-info-item">
                                <span class="up-info-label">Address</span>
                                <span class="up-info-value">@profile?.Address</span>
                            </li>
                        }
                    </ul>
                </div>

                @* ── BECOME A SELLER BUTTON ── *@
                @if (profile?.Role != "Seller" && profile?.Role != "Admin")
                {
                    <div class="up-filter-group" style="margin-top: 20px; padding-top: 16px; border-top: 1px solid var(--c-border);">
                        <a asp-controller="User" asp-action="Requests" class="up-btn up-btn--primary" style="width: 100%; justify-content: center; gap: 8px;">
                            <svg width="18" height="18" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2">
                                <path d="M12 5v14M5 12h14" />
                            </svg>
                            Become a Seller
                        </a>
                        <p class="up-form-hint" style="margin-top: 10px; text-align: center; font-size: 0.75rem;">
                            Start selling your items to thousands of buyers
                        </p>

                        @if (sellerApp != null && sellerApp.Status == ApplicationStatus.Pending)
                        {
                            <div class="up-alert up-alert--info" style="margin-top: 16px; padding: 10px; font-size: 0.75rem;">
                                <svg width="14" height="14" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2">
                                    <circle cx="12" cy="12" r="10" />
                                    <polyline points="12 6 12 12 16 14" />
                                </svg>
                                <span>Seller application pending review</span>
                            </div>
                        }
                        else if (sellerApp != null && sellerApp.Status == ApplicationStatus.Rejected)
                        {
                            <div class="up-alert up-alert--warning" style="margin-top: 16px; padding: 10px; font-size: 0.75rem;">
                                <svg width="14" height="14" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2">
                                    <circle cx="12" cy="12" r="10" />
                                    <line x1="12" y1="8" x2="12" y2="12" />
                                    <line x1="12" y1="16" x2="12.01" y2="16" />
                                </svg>
                                <span>Previous application rejected — you can reapply</span>
                            </div>
                        }
                    </div>
                }
                else if (profile?.Role == "Seller")
                {
                    <div class="up-filter-group" style="margin-top: 20px; padding-top: 16px; border-top: 1px solid var(--c-border);">
                        <a asp-controller="Shop" asp-action="Index" class="up-btn up-btn--primary" style="width: 100%; justify-content: center; gap: 8px;">
                            <svg width="18" height="18" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2">
                                <rect x="3" y="4" width="18" height="18" rx="2" ry="2" />
                                <line x1="16" y1="2" x2="16" y2="6" />
                                <line x1="8" y1="2" x2="8" y2="6" />
                                <line x1="3" y1="10" x2="21" y2="10" />
                            </svg>
                            Manage Your Shop
                        </a>
                    </div>
                }
            </aside>

    <script>
        (function () {
            'use strict';

            var input   = document.getElementById('amountInput');
            var form    = document.getElementById('addFundsForm');
            var btn     = document.getElementById('addFundsBtn');
            var presets = document.querySelectorAll('.addfunds-quick__btn');

            presets.forEach(function (p) {
                p.addEventListener('click', function () {
                    if (!input) return;
                    input.value = p.dataset.amount;
                    presets.forEach(function (b) { b.classList.remove('addfunds-quick__btn--active'); });
                    p.classList.add('addfunds-quick__btn--active');
                });
            });

            if (input) {
                input.addEventListener('input', function () {
                    presets.forEach(function (b) { b.classList.remove('addfunds-quick__btn--active'); });
                    presets.forEach(function (b) {
                        if (b.dataset.amount === input.value) b.classList.add('addfunds-quick__btn--active');
                    });
                });
            }

            if (form && btn) {
                form.addEventListener('submit', function () {
                    btn.disabled = true;
                    btn.textContent = 'Processing…';
                });
            }
        }());
    </script>
}

            else
            {
                <div class="wlt-tx-list">
                    @foreach (var tx in Model.RecentTransactions)
                    {
                        // Determine if this transaction is a credit (money coming IN to the current user/rider)
                        bool isCredit;
                        
                        if (isRider)
                        {
                            // For riders: credit if ToRiderId matches current user
                            isCredit = tx.ToRiderId == Model.CurrentUserId
                                && tx.Type != TransactionType.EscrowHold
                                && tx.Type != TransactionType.Withdrawal;
                        }
                        else
                        {
                            // For regular users: credit if ToUserId matches current user
                            isCredit = tx.ToUserId == Model.CurrentUserId
                                && tx.Type != TransactionType.EscrowHold
                                && tx.Type != TransactionType.Withdrawal;
                        }
                        
                        bool isDebit = !isCredit;

                        string typeLabel = tx.Type switch
                        {
                            TransactionType.EscrowHold => "Escrow Hold",
                            TransactionType.EscrowRelease => "Escrow Release",
                            TransactionType.Withdrawal => "Withdrawal",
                            TransactionType.CashCollection => "Cash Collected",
                            TransactionType.TopUp => "Funds Added",
                            TransactionType.DeliveryFeePayment => "Delivery Fee",

                            TransactionType.EscrowRelease => "unlock",
                            TransactionType.Withdrawal => "arrow-up",
                            TransactionType.CashCollection => "cash",
                            TransactionType.TopUp => "plus",
                            TransactionType.DeliveryFeePayment => "delivery",
                            _ => "dot"
                        };

                                }
                                else if (typeIcon == "unlock")
                                {
                                    <svg viewBox="0 0 20 20" fill="currentColor" width="16" height="16"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M14.5 1A4.5 4.5 0 0010 5.5V9H3a2 2 0 00-2 2v6a2 2 0 002 2h10a2 2 0 002-2v-6a2 2 0 00-2-2h-1.5V5.5a3 3 0 116 0v2.75a.75.75 0 001.5 0V5.5A4.5 4.5 0 0014.5 1z" clip-rule="evenodd" /></svg>
                                }
                                else if (typeIcon == "arrow-up")

                                }
                                else if (typeIcon == "cash")

            .wd-amount-wrap:focus-within {
                border-color: var(--color-primary, #2d5a27);
            }

        .wd-amount-wrap__sym {
            padding: 0 0.875rem;
            font-family: 'DM Sans', sans-serif;
            font-size: 1.1rem;
            color: var(--color-muted, #8a8278);
            border-right: 1.5px solid var(--color-border, #e2ddd6);
        }

        .wd-amount-input {
            flex: 1;
            border: none;
            outline: none;
            padding: 0.875rem;
            font-family: 'DM Serif Display', serif;
            font-size: 1.5rem;
            color: var(--color-text, #1a1814);
            background: transparent;
            width: 100%;
        }

        .wd-all-btn {
            background: none;
            border: none;
            padding: 0;
            font-family: 'DM Sans', sans-serif;
            font-size: 0.8125rem;
            color: var(--color-primary, #2d5a27);
            cursor: pointer;
            text-decoration: underline;
            text-align: left;
        }

        .wd-method-group {
            display: flex;
            flex-direction: column;
            gap: 0.625rem;
        }

        .wd-method-option {
            display: flex;
            align-items: center;
            gap: 0.875rem;
            padding: 0.875rem 1rem;
            border: 1.5px solid var(--color-border, #e2ddd6);
            border-radius: 10px;
            background: #fff;
            cursor: pointer;
            transition: border-color 0.15s, background 0.15s;
        }

            .wd-method-option:hover,
            .wd-method-option--active {
                border-color: var(--color-primary, #2d5a27);
                background: color-mix(in srgb, var(--color-primary, #2d5a27) 4%, transparent);
            }

        .wd-method-radio {
            display: none;
        }

        .wd-method-option__icon {
            width: 36px;
            height: 36px;
            border-radius: 8px;
            background: color-mix(in srgb, var(--color-primary, #2d5a27) 10%, transparent);
            color: var(--color-primary, #2d5a27);
            display: flex;
            align-items: center;
            justify-content: center;
            flex-shrink: 0;
        }

        .wd-method-option__name {
            font-family: 'DM Sans', sans-serif;
            font-size: 0.9rem;
            font-weight: 600;
            color: var(--color-text, #1a1814);
            margin: 0 0 1px;
        }

        .wd-method-option__hint {
            font-family: 'DM Sans', sans-serif;
            font-size: 0.78rem;
            color: var(--color-muted, #8a8278);
            margin: 0;
        }

        .wd-submit {
            width: 100%;
            justify-content: center;
        }
    </style>

    <script>
        (function () {
            'use strict';

            var amountInput = document.getElementById('amountInput');
            var allBtn      = document.getElementById('withdrawAllBtn');
            var wdForm      = document.getElementById('wdForm');
            var wdSubmitBtn = document.getElementById('wdSubmitBtn');
            var methodRadios = document.querySelectorAll('.wd-method-radio');
            var methodLabels = document.querySelectorAll('.wd-method-option');

            // "Withdraw all" shortcut
            if (allBtn && amountInput) {
                allBtn.addEventListener('click', function () {
                    amountInput.value = amountInput.max;
                });
            }

            // Sync method option visual state with radio selection
            methodRadios.forEach(function (radio, i) {
                radio.addEventListener('change', function () {
                    methodLabels.forEach(function (lbl) { lbl.classList.remove('wd-method-option--active'); });
                    if (radio.checked) methodLabels[i].classList.add('wd-method-option--active');
                });
            });

            // Update reference hint based on method
            var referenceHint = document.getElementById('referenceHint');
            methodRadios.forEach(function (radio) {
                radio.addEventListener('change', function () {
                    if (!referenceHint) return;
                    referenceHint.textContent = radio.value === '1'
                        ? 'Your preferred pickup location or reference code.'
                        : 'Your bank account number or preferred pickup reference.';
                });
            });

            // Disable submit while in-flight
            if (wdForm && wdSubmitBtn) {
                wdForm.addEventListener('submit', function () {
                    wdSubmitBtn.disabled = true;
                    wdSubmitBtn.textContent = 'Submitting…';
                });
            }
        }());
    </script>
}


--- wwwroot/js/map-picker.js ---
// wwwroot/js/map-picker.js
// Leaflet + OpenStreetMap address picker.
// Reverse-geocoding via Nominatim (no API key required).
// ------------------------------------------------------------------
// Public API (called from inline onclick / _AddressInputWithMap):
//   openMapPicker(inputId)   – opens the modal targeting <inputId>
//   confirmMapAddress()      – copies preview into target input & closes
//   closeMapPicker()         – closes the modal without saving
//   searchMapAddress()       – geocodes the search-box query
// ------------------------------------------------------------------

(function () {
    'use strict';

    /* ── State ──────────────────────────────────────────────────── */
    let map = null;
    let marker = null;
    let targetId = null;   // id of the textarea we are filling
    let userCallback = null; // optional callback passed by caller
    let altTextId = null; // optional id of a visible text input to use for forward geocoding
    let geocodeCtrl = null;   // AbortController for in-flight fetch
    let mapInitialized = false;
    let allowEdit = true; // when false, map is view-only (no placing/draggable)

    /* ── DOM helpers ────────────────────────────────────────────── */
    const $ = id => document.getElementById(id);

    function setSpinner(on) {
        const el = $('map-geocode-spinner');
        if (el) el.classList.toggle('is-loading', on);
    }

    function setPreview(text) {
        const el = $('map-picker-address-preview');
        if (el) el.value = text;
    }

    function showPinpointPreview(lat, lng) {
        // Hide editing UI when viewing-only
        const confirmBtn = $('map-picker-confirm-btn');
        if (confirmBtn) confirmBtn.style.display = 'none';
        const searchWrapper = $('map-picker-search-wrapper');
        if (searchWrapper) searchWrapper.style.display = 'none';
        const footer = $('map-picker-footer');
        if (footer) footer.style.justifyContent = 'flex-end';
        // preview text will be filled by reverseGeocode; leave it intact otherwise
    }

    /* ── Map initialisation ─────────────────────────────────────── */

    function initMap() {
        const mapContainer = $('map-picker-map');

        // Check if container actually has dimensions
        if (!mapContainer || mapContainer.clientHeight === 0) {
            console.warn('[map-picker] Map container has zero height. Retrying...');
            setTimeout(initMap, 50);
            return;
        }

        if (map) {
            // Already initialised — invalidate size to recalculate tiles
            map.invalidateSize();
            // If a marker exists, ensure we pan to it so the user sees the selected location
            setTimeout(() => {
                try {
                    map.invalidateSize();
                    if (marker) {
                        map.panTo(marker.getLatLng());
                    }
                } catch (err) { /* ignore */ }
            }, 100);
            return;
        }

        // Default centre: Manila, Philippines
        map = L.map('map-picker-map', {
            zoomControl: true,
            attributionControl: true
        }).setView([14.5995, 120.9842], 13);

        L.tileLayer('https://{s}.tile.openstreetmap.org/{z}/{x}/{y}.png', {
            attribution: '&copy; <a href="https://www.openstreetmap.org/copyright" target="_blank">OpenStreetMap</a> contributors',
            maxZoom: 19
        }).addTo(map);

        map.on('click', onMapClick);

        mapInitialized = true;
        console.log('[map-picker] Map initialized successfully');
    }

    /* ── Map interactions ───────────────────────────────────────── */

    function onMapClick(e) {
        if (!allowEdit) return;
        placeMarker(e.latlng.lat, e.latlng.lng);
        reverseGeocode(e.latlng.lat, e.latlng.lng);
    }

    function placeMarker(lat, lng) {
        if (marker) {
            marker.setLatLng([lat, lng]);
        } else {
            marker = L.marker([lat, lng], { draggable: allowEdit }).addTo(map);
            if (allowEdit) {
                marker.on('dragend', function () {
                    const pos = marker.getLatLng();
                    reverseGeocode(pos.lat, pos.lng);
                });
            }
        }
        map.panTo([lat, lng]);
        // Write coordinates to the hidden inputs associated with the current target
        if (targetId) {
            const latEl = $(targetId + '-latitude');
            const lngEl = $(targetId + '-longitude');
            if (latEl) latEl.value = lat.toFixed(6);
            if (lngEl) lngEl.value = lng.toFixed(6);
            // If view-only, also show pinpoint preview
            if (!allowEdit) showPinpointPreview(lat, lng);
        }
    }

    /* ── Geocoding ──────────────────────────────────────────────── */

    /**
     * Nominatim reverse geocode: coords → address string.
     */
    function reverseGeocode(lat, lng) {
        // Cancel any previous in-flight request
        if (geocodeCtrl) geocodeCtrl.abort();
        geocodeCtrl = new AbortController();

        setSpinner(true);
        setPreview('Fetching address…');

        fetch(
            `https://nominatim.openstreetmap.org/reverse?lat=${lat}&lon=${lng}&format=json`,
            {
                headers: { 'Accept-Language': 'en' },
                signal: geocodeCtrl.signal
            }
        )
            .then(r => {
                if (!r.ok) throw new Error('Network error');
                return r.json();
            })
            .then(data => {
                setPreview(data.display_name ?? '');
            })
            .catch(err => {
                if (err.name !== 'AbortError') {
                    setPreview('');
                    console.warn('[map-picker] Reverse geocode failed:', err);
                }
            })
            .finally(() => setSpinner(false));
    }

    /**
     * Nominatim forward geocode: address string → coords.
     * Called when the user types in the search box and hits Search.
     */
    function geocodeQuery(query) {
        if (!query.trim()) return;
        if (geocodeCtrl) geocodeCtrl.abort();
        geocodeCtrl = new AbortController();

        setSpinner(true);

        fetch(
            `https://nominatim.openstreetmap.org/search?q=${encodeURIComponent(query)}&format=json&limit=1`,
            {
                headers: { 'Accept-Language': 'en' },
                signal: geocodeCtrl.signal
            }
        )
            .then(r => r.json())
            .then(data => {
                if (!data.length) {
                    alert('Address not found. Try a more specific query.');
                    return;
                }
                const lat = parseFloat(data[0].lat);
                const lng = parseFloat(data[0].lon);

                // Ensure map is initialized before using
                if (map) {
                    map.setView([lat, lng], 17);
                    placeMarker(lat, lng);
                    reverseGeocode(lat, lng);
                } else {
                    console.warn('[map-picker] Map not ready yet for geocode');
                }
            })
            .catch(err => {
                if (err.name !== 'AbortError')
                    console.warn('[map-picker] Forward geocode failed:', err);
            })
            .finally(() => setSpinner(false));
    }

    /* ── Pre-populate helper ────────────────────────────────────── */

    /**
     * If the target textarea already holds a value when the modal opens,
     * forward-geocode it so the map centres on the current address.
     */
    function tryPrePopulate(inputId) {
        // If coordinates hidden inputs exist, use them to position the marker
        const latEl = $(inputId + '-latitude');
        const lngEl = $(inputId + '-longitude');
        const existing = ($(inputId)?.value ?? '').trim();

        const tryMap = () => {
            if (!map) {
                setTimeout(tryMap, 100);
                return;
            }

            if (latEl && lngEl && latEl.value && lngEl.value) {
                const lat = parseFloat(latEl.value);
                const lng = parseFloat(lngEl.value);
                if (!isNaN(lat) && !isNaN(lng)) {
                    map.setView([lat, lng], 17);
                    placeMarker(lat, lng);
                    reverseGeocode(lat, lng);
                    return;
                }
            }

            if (existing) {
                geocodeQuery(existing);
            }
        };

        tryMap();
    }

    /* ── Public API ─────────────────────────────────────────────── */

    /**
     * Open the map picker targeting the <textarea id="inputId">.
     */
    // signature: openMapPicker(inputId, [callbackOrAlt], [mode])
    window.openMapPicker = function (inputId, secondArg, mode) {
        // Support optional second arg: a callback function to receive (latLng, addressString)
        targetId = inputId;
        userCallback = null;
        altTextId = null;
        if (typeof secondArg === 'function') userCallback = secondArg;
        if (typeof secondArg === 'string') altTextId = secondArg;

        // determine view-only vs editable mode early so pre-population uses correct behaviour
        allowEdit = true;
        if (typeof mode === 'string' && mode === 'view') allowEdit = false;
        if (!allowEdit && marker && marker.dragging) {
            try { marker.dragging.disable(); } catch (e) { /* ignore */ }
        }

        const overlay = $('map-picker-modal');
        if (!overlay) {
            console.error('[map-picker] Modal element #map-picker-modal not found.');
            return;
        }

        // Reset search box
        const searchBox = $('map-picker-search');
        if (searchBox) searchBox.value = '';

        overlay.classList.add('is-open');

        // Wait for the modal's CSS transition to complete (0.22s)
        // before initializing the map to ensure the container has dimensions
        setTimeout(() => {
            initMap();
            // Pre-populate; tryPrePopulate will use hidden lat/lng inputs if present
            tryPrePopulate(inputId);
            // If view-only and coords exist, ensure UI reflects view-only immediately
            if (!allowEdit) {
                const latEl = $(inputId + '-latitude');
                const lngEl = $(inputId + '-longitude');
                if (latEl && lngEl && latEl.value && lngEl.value) {
                    const lat = parseFloat(latEl.value);
                    const lng = parseFloat(lngEl.value);
                    if (!isNaN(lat) && !isNaN(lng)) {
                        // ensure marker placed and map centered
                        placeMarker(lat, lng);
                        showPinpointPreview(lat, lng);
                    }
                }
            }
            // After a short delay ensure map repaint and marker centering
            setTimeout(() => {
                try {
                    if (map) map.invalidateSize();
                    const latEl = $(inputId + '-latitude');
                    const lngEl = $(inputId + '-longitude');
                    if (map && marker == null && latEl && lngEl && latEl.value && lngEl.value) {
                        const lat = parseFloat(latEl.value);
                        const lng = parseFloat(lngEl.value);
                        if (!isNaN(lat) && !isNaN(lng)) {
                            map.setView([lat, lng], 17);
                            placeMarker(lat, lng);
                            // ensure preview populated for view-only
                            if (!allowEdit) reverseGeocode(lat, lng);
                        }
                    } else if (map && marker) {
                        map.panTo(marker.getLatLng());
                        // if view-only, refresh preview from marker
                        if (!allowEdit) {
                            const pos = marker.getLatLng();
                            showPinpointPreview(pos.lat, pos.lng);
                            reverseGeocode(pos.lat, pos.lng);
                        }
                    }
                } catch (err) { /* ignore */ }
            }, 200);
        }, 250);
    };

    /**
     * Forward-geocode whatever is in the search input.
     * Wired to the Search button inside the modal.
     */
    window.searchMapAddress = function () {
        const q = ($('map-picker-search')?.value ?? '').trim();
        if (q) geocodeQuery(q);
    };

    /**
     * Confirm selection: copy preview text into the target textarea, then close.
     */
    window.confirmMapAddress = function () {
        const preview = ($('map-picker-address-preview')?.value ?? '').trim();
        if (preview && targetId) {
            const target = $(targetId);
            if (target) {
                target.value = preview;

                // Fire a native 'input' event so frameworks/validation pick up the change
                target.dispatchEvent(new Event('input', { bubbles: true }));
                target.dispatchEvent(new Event('change', { bubbles: true }));

                // Also ensure hidden fields are updated (in case marker was placed but not dragged)
                const latEl = $(targetId + '-latitude');
                const lngEl = $(targetId + '-longitude');
                if (marker && latEl && lngEl) {
                    const pos = marker.getLatLng();
                    latEl.value = pos.lat.toFixed(6);
                    lngEl.value = pos.lng.toFixed(6);
                }
            }
        }
        // If caller provided a callback, invoke it with selected coords and preview text
        try {
            if (userCallback && marker) {
                const pos = marker.getLatLng();
                userCallback({ lat: pos.lat, lng: pos.lng }, preview);
            }
        } catch (err) {
            console.warn('[map-picker] user callback threw:', err);
        }

        closeMapPicker();
    };

    /**
     * Close the modal without saving anything.
     */
    window.closeMapPicker = function () {
        const overlay = $('map-picker-modal');
        if (overlay) overlay.classList.remove('is-open');

        // Cancel any pending geocode request
        if (geocodeCtrl) {
            geocodeCtrl.abort();
            geocodeCtrl = null;
        }

        setSpinner(false);
        // clear optional callback so it doesn't leak between opens
        userCallback = null;
    };

    /* ── Keyboard support ───────────────────────────────────────── */

    document.addEventListener('keydown', function (e) {
        if (e.key === 'Escape') {
            const overlay = $('map-picker-modal');
            if (overlay && overlay.classList.contains('is-open')) closeMapPicker();
        }
    });

    // Allow pressing Enter in the search box to trigger search
    document.addEventListener('keydown', function (e) {
        if (e.key === 'Enter' && document.activeElement?.id === 'map-picker-search') {
            e.preventDefault();
            window.searchMapAddress();
        }
    });

    /* ── Click-outside-to-close ─────────────────────────────────── */

    document.addEventListener('click', function (e) {
        const overlay = $('map-picker-modal');
        if (overlay && overlay.classList.contains('is-open') && e.target === overlay) {
            closeMapPicker();
        }
    });

})();

--- wwwroot/js/site.js ---
// Please see documentation at https://learn.microsoft.com/aspnet/core/client-side/bundling-and-minification
// for details on configuring this project to bundle and minify static web assets.

// Write your JavaScript code.
